The defense of Tianjin is still being undertaken by the Tenth Regiment of the Sixty-Third Brigade of Yu's army. (September 26th)

First Step in the Campaign Against Lu to be Completed

Lu Xingming Expresses His Surrender

Fuzhou Correspondence: Qian Yuguang of Lu's troops recently expressed his surrender to the provincial authorities and took up the position of Brigade Commander of the Provisional Provincial Defense First Brigade in Gutian. However, when Lin Shouguo's troops arrived at Daqiaotou, which is under Gutian's jurisdiction, Zhang Chunguang, Qian's deputy regimental commander, acted evasively, and they did not dare to advance rashly, entering the city only on the evening of the 23rd. Chen Heling's and Zhang Ziming's troops also sent personnel to the province yesterday to request incorporation. It is reported that the authorities have already approved, but the title is still being discussed. Lu Xingrong, seeing that the general situation was unfavorable, has moved his headquarters to the Majun Temple near Zhanghuban, to plan a retreat into Youxi. Zhou Zhiqún also led his troops to retreat to Shuikou. The Central Column of the Liu Division therefore advanced rapidly, generally taking Gutian with the land force, Chen Wantai taking Dahu from Beiling, Liu Shangzhi moving along the left bank of the Minjiang River, from Ganzhe, Baisha, and Daxiaoruo towards Shuikou, and Gui Zhenyuan moving along the right bank of the Minjiang River, taking Minqing from Houguan City. The first step of the plan against Lu will thus be completed. Lu Xingming, who went to Shanghai several months ago and has not returned, is the Brigade Commander of the First Brigade of Lu's troops. Yesterday, he telegraphed Fang Shengtao, stating that he was not involved in the January 6th Coup and that this war was purely instigated by one or two treacherous individuals. He is willing to return to Yanping to clean up the mess and await dispatch by the provincial authorities, and will send the six people he detained to the province immediately to atone for his sins, etc. Fang's visit to the province this time is to negotiate this issue with various parties, but the outcome is difficult to predict.

Another report states that Fang Shengtao's mission to the province this time is approximately threefold: (1) Funding: After Yang Shuzhuang and He Gonggan negotiated, it was decided that the counties of Jinnan and Hui would allocate funds, and another sum would be raised and handed over to Fang for use at the front; (2) Weapons and ammunition: A large batch of ammunition needed by the Chen Guohui, Wang Zuqing, Lin Qinglong, and Training Regiment, etc., of the southern Fujian army participating in the battle, will also be allocated by the arsenal and handed over to Fang; (3) Combat plan: The eastern route army's central, left, and right wings have all advanced in sequence. After meeting with Fang, Yan Er'ai rushed to the front yesterday (the 25th) with the general attack order, commanding Chen Wantai's and Liu Shangzhi's brigades to advance rapidly. Lin Shouguo also ordered Qian Yuguang to set out towards Shuikou. Lin Bingzhou's regiment will advance after Qian's troops, taking a connection with the central column. Fang decided to take the Xiamen round tomorrow to return to his post and has telegraphed the various units at the front to attack Datian in two routes from Fangtengkeng Longhusi. (September 26th)

Another report states that the troops of the Lu Xingrong, Lu Xinming, and Zhou Zhiqún three brigades of Lu's troops in the area along the Minjiang River from Fuzhou to Yanping, including Ganzhe, Zhuqi, Baisha, Guanyuan, Dahu, Muyuan Ruoyang, Jiangyang, Anren, and Xuefeng, have gradually retreated after being attacked by the Liu Division. There is no trace of Lu's troops in the western suburbs of Fuzhou. The vanguard of Liu Shangzhi's brigade has now entered Minqing, and the vanguard of Chen Wantai's brigade has entered Yongtai. The Marine Corps Lin Shouguo's brigade has also entered Gutian. The first step of the military operation has been completed, and the second step is to attack Yanping. However, after Lu's troops withdrew from the western suburbs of Fuzhou, they used all their strength to defend the Shuikou area, which is a vital passage from the province to Yanping, and used the dangerous terrain with mountains on three sides and water on one side to build defensive works to block the provincial army's advance northward. On the 25th, after Yan Er'ai went to the front line to supervise the battle, he used Lin's brigade in coordination with Qian Yuguang's troops, Chen's brigade in coordination with Liang Jichuan's troops, and Liu's brigade in coordination with Huang Bingwu's troops, to launch a general attack on Shuikou in three routes from convenient paths, with Gui's brigade serving as the general reserve force in the rear. Contact began on the 26th, and there will be a fierce battle. As for the military situation in southern Fujian, Fang Shengtao has completed discussions with Yang Shuzhuang and Liu Heding in the province and will return to his post to command the various armies to attack Youxi from Dehua and Datian, to coordinate with the Fuzhou army, as soon as the funding and ammunition are received. Due to the large-scale offensive launched by the provincial army on both the east and west routes, Lu Fang has transferred all his troops to the front line to resist, leaving the rear extremely empty. There is only one regiment of garrison troops in Jianning and Shaowu, and bandits are rising up everywhere. Yanping has been alarmed several times in one night. All valuables and direct relatives have been moved back to the Sixth Capital of Youxi and stored in caves to avoid air raids. Furthermore, Chen Heling's and Zhang Ziming's two regiments, formerly under Chen Rongbiao, have surrendered to the provincial authorities and have retreated from Gutian into Luoyuan. Finally, news was received that Shuikou was captured this morning (the 27th), with Liu Shangzhi's brigade being the first to enter. Lu's troops retreated to Zhanghuban, on the border between Minqing and Yanping, and Liu's brigade is in pursuit. Yang Shuzhuang and Liu Heding have now ordered Lin Shouguo's and Chen Wantai's brigades to continue straight to Yanping. (September 27th)

Guangdong Provincial Regulations Restore Branch Offices in Various Prefectures

Unredeemed Banknotes Rise to Over Ninety Percent

Guangzhou Correspondence: Recently, Guangdong's financial situation has been slightly more active than before. The biggest reason for this is that the financial treasury bonds issued a few days ago have been gradually delivered. According to news from the Finance Department yesterday, various collection agencies and groups in various places have remitted two to three million yuan in cash, in addition to branch treasuries. This has been transferred to the Central Bank for the purpose of redeeming unredeemed banknotes. On the 24th, the Central Bank convened a board meeting to discuss ways to restore various unredeemed banknotes. Attendees that day included directors Fan Qiwu, Jin Cengcheng, Lin Yunhai, and Shen Zaihe. The meeting opened at 2:00 p.m., with Governor Qu Guokang reporting on the Central Bank's business income and expenditure situation over the years. Next, the reorganization of the Central Bank's business and the plan to restore the business of branch offices in various places were discussed. The meeting adjourned at approximately 4:00 p.m. The Central Bank's Nanlu and Beihai Meilu branch offices have been forced to cease operations since the outbreak of the war in Guangxi Province, as Nanlu is connected to Guangxi and has been repeatedly ravaged by the enemy. The Central Bank has been increasingly well-funded recently, and the two branches cannot be allowed to remain closed for long. Therefore, at the board meeting that day, it was proposed that they be restored as soon as possible. A certain Yu, the director of the Beihai Central Bank branch office, arrived in the province yesterday to report on preparations for the resumption of business. At the same time, the Meilu branch office also sent a telegram to the province, stating that it could open during the day. It is now waiting for the provincial bank to send cash. After receiving the report, the Central Bank has prepared to dispatch a warship to transport tens of thousands of cash first, so that the two branches can allocate funds for resumption of business. If cash is delivered during the day, the two branches may be able to resume business on October 1st. While restoring branch offices, the Central Bank is also preparing to resume redemption. At the same time, the demand for unredeemed banknotes is increasing due to the payment of financial treasury bonds. Therefore, the value of unredeemed five-yuan and ten-yuan banknotes has risen daily. On the 24th, the market value at the entrance was 906, and the market value at the exit was 914. Based on this trend, there may be hope for continued gains. According to Finance Department Director Fan Qiwu, the timing of the resumption of redemption of unredeemed five-yuan and ten-yuan banknotes is a matter of financial secrecy and cannot be announced for the time being. In short, the war between the North and South is coming to an end, and the Central Bank's resumption of redemption will be as easy as turning one's hand. At present, the Central Bank has prepared seven to eight million yuan in funds and can announce redemption at any time. There are only over ten million yuan of unredeemed banknotes in the market these days, including less than one million yuan of unredeemed fifty-yuan notes. The remaining ten-yuan and five-yuan notes have increased in value recently due to increased demand, which is really what is expected. (September 26th)

Bengbu News Regarding the Reorganization of the Anhui Provincial Government

New Provincial Committee Takes Office on Schedule

Yue Shengxuan's Division Enters Anhui First

Bengbu Correspondence: The reorganization of the Anhui Provincial Government has been announced for many days. The newly appointed Provincial Government Chairman Chen Diaoyuan is still in Liuhe due to military affairs and has not been able to come to Anhui. The new provincial committee members, such as Civil Affairs Director Zhu Xi, Finance Director Yuan Jiapu, and Construction Director Chen Luanshu, have arrived in Beijing for many days. In the past, due to the financial problems of Anhui Province and the methods of dispatching troops to suppress bandits, it was necessary to consult with the central government in the long term. Therefore, the trip was delayed. Now that concrete measures have been determined for each item, it has been decided to go to Anhui to take office in the next few days. The provincial government has sent special commissioners to Beijing to welcome them. It is reported that Zhu and others have set the 1st of next month to take office. It is not yet certain whether Chen Diaoyuan will go to Anhui at present. According to people in Chen's general headquarters, his first policy for governing Anhui is to start by clearing out bandits. In addition to the Fan Xiji and other divisions at the front, Chen's directly subordinate troops have recently established the Fifty-Seventh Division, commanded by Yue Shengxuan, courtesy name Ming San, from Dantu, Jiangsu. Yue is Chen's old subordinate, originally a battalion commander, who has been promoted over the years to his current position. The Song Runtian and Liang Hongen brigades are both under the division's command. Song's troops are in Xuzhou, organized as the 169th Brigade, and Liang's troops are in Tengxian, organized as the 170th Brigade. Yue personally reviewed them separately a few days ago. Chen Diaoyuan believed that the division was well-trained and ordered it to enter Anhui as the basic force for suppressing bandits and garrisoning. Liang's brigade first set out southward from Tengxian. On the 25th, Liang Hongen arrived in Xuzhou, entered the city to visit Division Commander Yue, and led his troops south by train that evening. At 4:00 a.m. on the 26th, the first battalion of the 340th Regiment of the brigade first passed Bengbu by train. At 6:00 a.m. on the 27th, Regiment Commander Yan of the 340th Regiment led the second battalion to pass Bengbu by train. At 8:00 a.m., the entire 339th Regiment passed Bengbu by train. At 9:00 p.m., Yue Shengxuan led the division headquarters officers and the entire 341st Regiment to pass Bengbu by train. As soon as the various units arrived at Pukou, they transferred to riverboats and went west to Anqing. After Liang's brigade set out, the defense of Tengxian that was left behind will be filled by Ma Hongkui's troops. (September 28th)

Extension of Time for Trade Union Reorganization for Three Months

Ministry of Industry and Commerce Notifies Various Provinces and Cities for Compliance

Minister of Industry and Commerce Kong Xiangxi previously submitted to the Executive Yuan that since the promulgation of the Trade Union Law and its Implementation Regulations, many trade unions in various places had not been newly established or merged and reorganized in accordance with the law, requesting a slight restriction. The Executive Yuan forwarded it to the National Government, which in turn forwarded it to the Central Party Headquarters. Subsequently, a reply was received, advocating that the reorganization of people's organizations be guided in accordance with the resolution of the 102nd Central Standing Committee, extending the time limit by three months. The State Council then approved and ordered compliance. After receiving the order, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce has notified the provincial and municipal governments a few days ago to comply. The text of the consultation is recorded as follows: "Since the promulgation of the Trade Union Law and its Implementation Regulations, many trade unions in various places have not been newly established or merged in accordance with the law, nor have they applied for an extension of time in accordance with the law. Not only does this hinder the effectiveness of the law, but it also increases administrative difficulties. Our ministry previously intended to slightly restrict the deadline for such registration and merger, and submitted a request to the Executive Yuan, which was forwarded to the National Government for approval. Now, within the Executive Yuan's 3362nd instruction, it is stated that the ministry's request to slightly restrict the deadline for the re-registration and merger of trade unions established before the implementation of the Trade Union Law and to notify the provinces and cities to comply within one month of receiving the document has been reported and instructed to be informed to the ministry. Now, within the National Government's instruction No. 508, it is stated that the ministry's request to restrict the deadline for the re-registration and merger of trade unions established before the implementation of the Trade Union Law and to notify the provinces and cities to comply within one month of receiving the document has been approved and requested to be forwarded to the Central Committee to order the compliance of all levels of party headquarters has been reported to the government, and it was resolved at the 88th State Council meeting to send it to the Central Party Headquarters for review. Now, within the Central Executive Committee's letter No. 13897, it is stated that the trade unions in various places have rarely re-registered or merged in accordance with the law. According to Article 24 of the Trade Union Law Implementation Regulations, the government should consider extending the deadline. However, the situations of trade unions in various places are not uniform. If in areas where military affairs have not yet ended and other areas with special circumstances, it seems too hasty to limit the completion to one month. It is found that the second article of the measures for guiding the reorganization of people's organizations passed by the 102nd Standing Committee of this conference states that 'Except as otherwise provided by laws and regulations, all party headquarters listed above must guide the reorganization of the people's organizations under their jurisdiction within three months of receiving these measures, but in special circumstances, they may apply to the training department of the Central Executive Committee for an extension level by level.' In order to facilitate the guidance of local party headquarters and the supervision of the government, it seems that the government should refer to the above resolution, order an extension of three months, and those with special circumstances may also apply for an extension. This is specially conveyed in this letter, hoping that you will check and handle it accordingly, etc. This was received, and it was immediately submitted to the 93rd State Council meeting of this government, and it was resolved to handle it accordingly. In addition to the fact that the measures for guiding people's organizations have been copied and circulated, it is ordered that the Executive Yuan should comply with and handle it accordingly, this order, etc. This was received, and it should be complied with and handled accordingly, and an order should be issued to the local competent authorities to order all trade unions in their respective districts to re-register or merge in accordance with the law within three months of receiving the document. Those with special circumstances should also promptly state the reasons for extending the deadline within three months and apply for approval in order to maintain the laws and regulations. In addition to distributing consultations, a corresponding consultation is requested for review and compliance by all subordinates."

Liaoning Province Prepares for National Day Parade

Shenyang Correspondence: Zhang Xueliang, Commander of the Northeast Border Defense, believes that the Double Tenth Festival this year is approaching. This day is the National Day Ceremony, and a military parade should be held to express celebration. He has now appointed Wang Yizhe, Brigade Commander of the First Brigade of the Northeast Army, to be responsible for preparations and has also appointed Wang as the temporary commander-in-chief of the parade ground. The units designated to participate in the parade are: (1) Infantry, consisting of two battalions of infantry from the First Brigade and special companies, organized into two infantry regiments; (2) Garrison Infantry, consisting of two battalions of infantry from the Garrison and special companies, organized into one infantry regiment; (3) Cavalry, consisting of the cavalry company of the First Brigade and a company sent by the cavalry of the Garrison, combined into one cavalry regiment; (4) Artillery, consisting of the Artillery Training Corps, organized into one artillery regiment; (5) Engineers, consisting of units drawn from the Engineer Training and Supervision Department, organized into one engineer battalion; (6) Tank Corps; (7) Searchlight Team; (8) Air Force; (9) Military Band. The flags, uniforms, equipment, and machinery of the above units will be inspected by the Commander-in-Chief in advance to ensure uniformity. The formation and order of the parade will also be determined by the Commander-in-Chief in advance and submitted to the Commander for approval. Other preparations for the venue and hospitality security matters have also been planned as follows: (1) All preparatory matters for the parade ground will be handled by the Deputy Adjutant Office of the Border Defense Headquarters; (2) Reception of guests: Foreign guests will be attended to by personnel from the Foreign Affairs Office, together with translators and secretaries from the Border Defense Headquarters. Domestic guests will be attended to by the Adjutant Office; (3) Guests are limited to foreign consuls, military attachés, representatives of overseas Chinese groups, senior military and political officials and representatives from domestic provinces and regions, and representatives of various organizations, legal entities, and citizens in this city; (4) The dress code for military officers accompanying the parade will be determined by the Adjutant Office; (5) Security of the parade ground will be provided by a squadron of military police dispatched by the Military Police Headquarters, under the temporary dispatch and deployment of the Commander-in-Chief; (6) Security along the route will be provided by Commander Chen Xingya of the Military Police, together with Commander Liu Duoquan of the Garrison and Director Bai Mingzhen of the Public Security Bureau, who will dispatch a certain number of military police, police, and guards to be properly deployed from the Commander's private residence to the parade ground. (September 25th)

Local Correspondence Songjiang

Sijing Robbery Case Lake Bandits Publicly Tried Sijing Town, in the county, was suddenly attacked by a large gang of lake bandits waving a flag with the character "Mao" on the afternoon of April 28th this year. The self-defense corps ran out of ammunition and had no reinforcements, and several people were killed or injured. Later, the troops and police of the neighboring Qingpu and Jiading counties intercepted the stolen goods and bandits involved in the case. The county government sent police to escort them separately. The county court was established and transferred the case to the court for investigation. The prosecutor's office has completed the investigation, finding that bandits Lin Zicheng, Xu Yubao, Wang Decai, Liu Zhizhong, Wang Quanyou, Zuo Jinchi, Zuo Gensheng, Wang Changyou, Hong Zuojiang, Mao Ziqing, Li Wenqing, Wu Zhiyi, Gui Xiaodi, Wu Jiyi, Gao Xuekui, Wu Zhiyu, Wang Shaoquan, Kong Lingchuan, Zhu Weiliu, Wu Hanying, Wang Yuqing, and Dong Dachuan, etc., gathered in the mountains and swamps, resisted government troops, formed large gangs, and engaged in robbery and murder. According to the Regulations on the Punishment of Bandits, Shen Wangshi and Shen Lushi should also be punished as principals for providing direct and important assistance. The prosecution is filed in accordance with Article 253 of the Code of Criminal Procedure. The court has scheduled a debate hearing for today (30th) and has appointed six volunteer lawyers, Zhang Baopei, Lu Longxiang, Ye Renzhou, Zheng Wenwang, Tinggan Qianjin, to appear in court to defend. The court opened at 10:00 a.m. this morning, with Judge Li of the Criminal Court presiding. The prosecutor appeared in court to prosecute. The interrogator called each bandit in turn for interrogation. The confessions were mostly evasive or admitted to being conscripted as boatmen, forced to row boats. The statements differed greatly from those made during the investigation. But their ferocious appearances were revealed in their eyebrows. However, because there are many bandits, it took all day to interrogate them one by one. At 5:10 p.m., the judge announced a ten-minute break before resuming the interrogation. After the interrogation, it was heard that the debate was over and a sentence would be pronounced immediately.

Fengxian

The Kidnapping Case at Jinhui Bridge is Solved. Last month, the family of Qian Guiqiu, a farmer in the 17th Tu of the 15th Bao in the Sixth District, had their eight-year-old grandson kidnapped by bandits. After receiving the report, the County Public Security Bureau, in addition to ordering the family not to privately negotiate a ransom, dispatched Inspector Chen Jinfang to Shanghai to assist in the investigation. It is now known that the bandits, seeing the strict security checkpoints, did not dare to insist. So they secretly abandoned the little hostage in a certain room of the Tianchan Hotel on Haining Road, to escape. Inspector Chen learned of the situation and, on the 25th of this month, joined forces with the local police station to rescue the child. The child was handed over to the family for identification yesterday.

The Excitement of Autumn Festival Commercial Auctions This county has suffered from years of scarcity, and commerce has been greatly affected. Fortunately, this year's flower and rice harvests are abundant, and the market is active. So all industries are taking advantage of this autumn harvest to launch auctions, which are currently being discounted to attract customers, and are very lively. Among them, the silk and satin and foreign goods industries are particularly prosperous.

Nantang River Works Committee Holds Meeting The Nantang River works in Nanqiao have caused complaints and lawsuits due to local dissatisfaction. So County Chief Shen convened the original Nantang River Works Committee yesterday to discuss solutions. The committee members expressed their opinions, agreeing that the project depends on the weather and is difficult to complete by human effort. However, the various accounts should be thoroughly audited, and the cases of continuing to collect river donations and repaying interest on loans should be discussed separately. Otherwise, relying on a single reimbursement form will be difficult to convince people. It has been decided to form another audit committee for further review.

Suzhou

Captain Du Dies of Serious Injuries: Du Jingwu, Acting Captain of the 14th Water Police Team of Wujiang, was sent to the city for medical treatment after being attacked by bandits. Mr. Du died of excessive blood loss at 10 p.m. on the 29th at the Bo Xi Hospital. It is reported that when the bandits attacked the team headquarters, they divided into two groups. One group surrounded the patrol boat in front of the team headquarters, and the other went to the headquarters, captured the guard, silenced him, and then went around to the back of the house. They fired guns from the window at Du's bed. Du was awakened from his dream and got out of bed to take his Mauser pistol and fired back out the window while calling the city for help. Eventually, he was shot four times by the dense bandit fire, and his bullets ran out. He crawled into the small courtyard behind the house to hide. The bandits saw that the gunfire in the house had stopped and rushed in to search. They found no one, so they took more than one hundred silver dollars and two Mauser pistols from the clothes chest. Four police officers were injured on the patrol boat, and more than ten guns were robbed.

Pig Boat Robbed En Route: Xu Hengda Pig Trade in the Cat Gate area sent Zhou Apan to Taixing, north of the Yangtze River, to transport pigs to Suzhou. At about 1 a.m. the day before yesterday, when passing the Shili Pavilion ferry area near Huguan, they were suddenly encountered by a bandit boat with about five or six bandits with a Hunan accent. Silver coins and clothing worth about three hundred yuan were robbed. Yesterday, Xu Kunquan, the owner of the trade, filed a report to the county to pursue the bandits.

Northeast Students Come to Suzhou for Inspection: Zhang Xueliang, President of Fengtian Northeastern University, specially dispatched two teams, a north team and a south team, for cultural inspection. The south team, led by Professor Xie Houfan, with more than 20 students, arrived in Suzhou yesterday from Wuxi and went to various schools to visit and tour the scenic spots. They are scheduled to take a train to Hangzhou tomorrow.

Jiang Jigui's Murder Portion Sentenced Not Guilty: Jiang Jigui, a worker at the Gongda Yarn Factory on Pingliang Road, Yangshupu, Shanghai, was sentenced to death on June 21 by the Shanghai District Court for a series of murders. Jiang refused to accept the judgment and appealed to the High Court. After several trials by Zheng Chi, the presiding judge of the Second Criminal Court, the sentence was pronounced yesterday (30th) at 3 p.m. The original judgment was revoked. Jiang Jigui was sentenced to three years of imprisonment for transporting bullets. After Jiang received the verdict, he no longer appealed because the death sentence had been revoked.

Wuxi

Continued Arrest of Main Thieves in Sun Lane Robbery Case: After the robbery of Sun Leikui's home in Sun Lane, the 12th and 13th Tu of the 16th District (Wananshi) of the county on August 5, the county police team successively captured three suspected thieves, He Genxi, He Genfu, and Yu Xingsheng, and sent them to the county for interrogation and detention. Xu Wencui, Director of the Public Security Bureau, recently received a secret report from the victim, Sun Leikui, stating that Sun Jiquan, a major thief in the case, was hiding in the countryside and requesting that police be dispatched to arrest him quickly. After receiving the report, Director Xu immediately dispatched a detective team to the countryside yesterday morning to investigate and arrest the suspect. Sun Jiquan was captured in the Yingqiao area and immediately arrested and sent to the bureau for interrogation.

Henan Refugees Disturb Wuxi: Recently, cases of unrest and robbery have emerged one after another, and the villagers are uneasy. Unexpectedly, at about 10 a.m. yesterday, more than 300 Henan refugees suddenly arrived at Zhongqiao Town in the Third District (Yangming Township). After arriving in the town, they forcibly demanded food from residents' shops. If they were not satisfied, they threatened and beat the villagers. Some of the refugees even held wooden sticks, bamboo poles, and other objects and rushed to the home of Chen Zhizhen, a doctor in the town, and carried out a large-scale robbery. Clothing and cash worth about one hundred yuan were robbed. Chen Zhizhen reported this to the Xiajiabian Public Security Eighth Branch, which sent police to suppress the situation and expel the refugees.

Selling His Wife for a Price and Falsely Accusing an Honest Man of Theft: Jin Arong, a native of Changzhou, lives on Guangqin Road outside Guangfu Gate in this county and makes a living by selling duck blood soup. His income is very meager, and he is extremely poor. Recently, Jin Arong found it increasingly difficult to make ends meet, so he painfully sold his wife, Ms. Mou, to Xu, a resident of Suzhou, to be his wife. At that time, the price was set at 130 yuan, with half of the price paid in advance. Unexpectedly, after Jin returned to Wuxi from Suzhou, Liao Dajin, the leader of the detective team of the county police brigade, learned that the money was of dubious origin and ordered his detectives to take Jin to a teahouse and accuse him of being a thief who robbed sweet potato boats. He was threatened in every possible way and subjected to torture. As a result, Jin paid 50 yuan to be released. Jin had no choice but to go to Suzhou again and ask the Xu family for the remaining half of the price of his wife, 65 yuan. Together with the previous 20 yuan, he had a total of 85 yuan, which he hid in his felt hat and took a car back to Wuxi. Unexpectedly, Liao Dajin sent his detectives to arrest him at the detective office and still accused him of being a thief. He was tortured with private punishment. Jin could not bear the torture and had to falsely confess. After Liao obtained the confession, he immediately presented it to the brigade headquarters. Yesterday, Brigade Commander Wang personally interrogated Jin Arong and learned that he was indeed an honest citizen who sold his wife due to poverty and was not a thief. Furthermore, Detective Team Leader Liao Dajin dared to use private punishment and falsely accuse an honest man of theft, which was extremely illegal. It is planned to submit a report to County Magistrate Pan for review.

###

Police and Bandits Clash at the Border of Wucheng: In Huangcun, about five or six miles from Longhutang in Wuyi County, there was a local defense corps. Due to the Xu Zixiang case last year, it was disbanded without a formal announcement, leaving dozens of firearms behind. Recently, bandits led by a high school student mistakenly heard that government police were coming to confiscate the weapons. Some of the bandits declared to the villagers on the night of the 28th that the firearms must not be handed over to the government police. They then went to the homes of Ni Maohai and Xu Guirong and confiscated three or four Mauser pistols. The Xishiqiao defense corps and the local police team learned about this and inquired that the bandit's secretary, Zhang Lupan, was hiding in Huangshu Village. They went there at dawn on the 29th and arrested him. When they escorted him to Huangcun Town, more than a hundred bandits suddenly came, each holding firearms and displaying military banners. They surrounded the police team and opened fire, causing a fierce exchange of gunfire between the two sides, resulting in deaths and injuries on both sides. Fortunately, police reinforcements from Shizhuang, Qiuzhuang, Ligang, and other areas arrived and continued the battle for two hours. The bandits were unable to withstand the pressure and fled westward. After investigation, it was found that Liu Quande on the bandit side was injured and fell to the ground, and Qian Zhengyuan, a shop assistant, was also shot and injured. Several police officers were injured, and several others were missing. This morning (30th), Cheng County dispatched another team to pursue and suppress the bandits.

Kidnapped Victim Zhu Fusheng Released: Zhu Fusheng, the son of Zhu Jinlin of Wujiaotou Village near Huangcun on the border of Wucheng, was kidnapped by bandits on the 26th, who demanded a ransom of 2,000 yuan. After various negotiations, Zhu Jinlin agreed to pay 480 yuan. On the 29th, he paid 200 yuan in advance, and the bandits released the victim. The remaining 280 yuan is due to be delivered on October 3rd.

Rampant Banditry in the Western Countryside: Banditry is rampant in Qianzhou, Huangcun, and other places in the western countryside. They are robbing firearms from local defense corps. Upon hearing this report, the Public Security Bureau investigated and found that the firearms of the Huangcun Street defense corps were undamaged, but six or seven were confiscated from the village. Xu Zixiang of Cunzhen was arrested and released. Xie Zuoming, the town chief of Xiejiatan, was kidnapped on the 28th. A police team was dispatched from the city to the countryside to join the Shizhuang police team and the Sixth District Defense Corps (including Ligang and Dingshi), totaling more than 60 people. They divided into two groups and surrounded Huangcun. At about 6 a.m. yesterday (29th), they opened fire with the bandits. Because they were outnumbered, they were surrounded. Bugler Lai Desheng was the first to be captured. Police officers Deng Yuqing and Zhao Guangqian, Cao Jitang (brother of Cao Zongduo, the district chief of the Eighth District of the Sixth Branch), and Zhao Jinyu and Geng Sangui of the Ligang Defense Corps are missing, and their life or death is unknown. Squad leader Li Jinshan was seriously injured and has been taken to the city for medical treatment. The police team retreated towards Yangtou Bridge. Three bandits were also killed. Two suspects, Wang Genda and Zhang Qizao (from Xiaohu), were arrested and sent to the county. The bandits, numbering about two or three hundred, are still entrenched in Huangcun, openly taking rice from the homes of civilians to cook meals. In the afternoon, Liu Zaigeng, the district chief of the Sixth District, went to the county government to report the emergency. In the evening, the garrison special operations company and the police team were dispatched to the countryside to suppress the bandits.

Zhenjiang

Setting Up Water Patrol Teams in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province: In order to rectify public security on the water, the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department has decided to set up water patrol teams in various counties. The existing water police teams will be reorganized. The temporary and recurring expenses will be determined by the county magistrates in accordance with the prescribed staffing levels from the local funds. The deadline for the establishment of the teams in each county is divided into three phases: the first phase is two months, the second phase is four months, and the third phase is six months.

Jiangsu Province Convenes Business Tax Conference: The Jiangsu Provincial Government has scheduled a preparatory meeting for business tax to be held at 2 p.m. on October 1 in the Finance Department, inviting representatives from the chambers of commerce of various counties. As of last night, representatives from Pizhou, Suqian, Siyang, and 22 other places have reported to the province. Representatives from the remaining 39 counties have already departed and should arrive in the province today. Most representatives believe that the collection of business tax should be implemented after the abolition of tariffs in accordance with the outline of the Five-Province Tariff Reduction Conference. Regarding the tax rate, the tax rate on domestic goods should be reduced, while the tax rate on imported goods may be increased. At 3 p.m. this afternoon, the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce will host a banquet for the representatives at the new building of the association and exchange opinions.

County Magistrates Must Have Military Knowledge: A total of 19 county magistrates were recruited in this session of Jiangsu Province, many of whom have served in social services for many years and have held county magistrate positions. However, county magistrates during the period of political tutelage are very important. Not only are experienced talents needed, but also considerable military knowledge is required to deal with everything. Therefore, the Civil Affairs Department is currently planning to establish a training institute for county magistrates to study military affairs. The duration is limited to two months.

Fourth Day of Teachers' Salary Demand: Yesterday at 6 p.m., teachers from various schools in the county town elected their principals to negotiate with the Education Bureau, but there was still no result. Therefore, this morning (28th) at 11 a.m., everyone gathered again at the First District First School to discuss the next steps: (1) It was resolved that since the Education Bureau had no intention of maintaining the teachers, everyone would unanimously resign from their respective schools and request that the owed salaries be paid in full so that they could find other means of living. (2) It was resolved to immediately issue a declaration of resignation to clarify the truth. (3) After resigning, if the principals could not fully pay the owed salaries, it was decided to invite the principals to demand payment from Acting Director Sun in person and not stop until the goal was achieved. After the discussion, You Zhangwu and Shen Shiru were mutually recommended to draft the declaration of resignation. Teachers also resigned from their respective principals.

Jiading

Provincial Order to Convert Chenjia Garden into a Park: Chenjia Garden in Nanxiang West City has been sealed for many years because the owner, Chen Zhigang, privately cast counterfeit money in the garden, and the case was discovered. Initially, the County Education Association requested that it be confiscated and allocated for local education. This was approved by the County Political Conference to sell its funds for the construction of the County Science Experiment Laboratory and reported to the provincial government for approval. Subsequently, the former Chanan Administrative Bureau requested that it be allocated as a bureau office. Recently, Nanxiang Public School requested that it be allocated as the school's campus. Various parties have different opinions, and the disputes are quite intense. The provincial government has negotiated with the Civil Affairs and Education Departments and intends to convert it into a park and provide civil and educational services. This was approved by the Provincial Government's 321st Committee Meeting and ordered the county to inform all parties.

Desperado Ma Zi Fude Arrested: Ma Zi Fude, a desperado formerly under the command of Tai Bao A Shu, a bandit leader, lived in Banlu Village and used to slaughter pigs in Qianjiawei. Recently, he gathered bandits in the area of Banlu Village to rob several families, including the Chen and Dai families in Xiaoxiquewei and the Zhou Fuorong family in Chaibaian. Recently, he also sent a letter to Shen Erhe's family, extorting 80 yuan. The New Cang Public Security Bureau learned of this on the 27th and discovered that the bandit was hiding in the home of his relative Zhang Xiaobao near Banlu Bridge. Director Xia immediately dispatched patrol leader Zhao and several police officers to arrest the bandit at the address. After Director Xia interrogated him, Fude confessed to the robbery without hesitation and also confessed the names of many accomplices. He has now been sent to the county government.

Autumn Cocoon Production This Year: Due to the failure to fully collect spring and summer cocoons in Zhejiang Province this year, many counties are supplementing with autumn silkworm rearing, which is more than double the amount of last year. The silk cocoons produced are also better than in previous years.

Meeting on Compensation Responsibility for Ping Tiao Losses: In the Shaoxing Ping Tiao case, the Grain Maintenance Association purchased rice at too high a price, which was not suitable for Ping Tiao. The rice was forcibly sold to rice shops in the city and countryside, resulting in a loss of more than 30,000 yuan of emergency grain reserves. The county convened an emergency meeting on the afternoon of the 29th.

Important News

President of National Jinan University

Zheng Hongnian Wishes to Specialize in Overseas Chinese Education

Submits Resignation from Political Deputy of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to the Executive Yuan

Zheng Hongnian, President of National Jinan University, submitted a proposal to the Executive Yuan yesterday, requesting to resign as Political Deputy of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and wishing to specialize in overseas Chinese education. The original submission stated,

In order to earnestly request permission to resign as Political Deputy of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, so as to devote oneself wholeheartedly to overseas Chinese education. Hongnian has been entrusted with a simple promotion and held a position as Political Deputy of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce. Although he has worked diligently, he is ultimately ashamed of having made no achievements. Upon recalling the overseas Chinese education that he advocated and founded twenty-three years ago, the mission has not yet been completed, and he is vigilant day and night, always concerned. In the spring of the sixteenth year, when the National Revolutionary Army settled in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, the various schools were suspended, and the music was temporarily stopped. The students of Jinan School requested Hongnian, who was the director when the school was established at the end of the Qing Dynasty, and who had used the nationalism revealed by the Premier's Tongmenghui as the meaning of the school song and set it as the educational policy, to take charge of the school administration. Hongnian advocated organizing a school affairs maintenance committee and recommended Li Shizeng, Wu Zhihui, Cai Yuanpei, and Hu Zhantang as committee members. Hongnian also intended to humbly occupy a seat and jointly plan the progress, and proposed a candidate. After several negotiations, the students all hoped for Hongnian. Hongnian's eldest daughter had just completed her studies and died prematurely, and his mood was bad, so the matter was abandoned and not discussed. The family did not let Hongnian know about the students' repeated requests. This was a polite refusal. Later, he learned that the students had gone directly to the former Central Education Administrative Committee to request that a receiver be sent first and then a principal be appointed. Public and private matters were intertwined, and Hongnian, although he himself judged that his talent and virtue were not worthy, dared not not reluctantly take on the arduous task. On June 14 of the sixteenth year, he arrived at the school to take over the matter, and thus, based on his long-held aspirations, reorganized the school affairs plan and reorganization, striving to improve the level of overseas Chinese children to adapt to the special environment overseas, hoping to academicize it and enable overseas Chinese elders to achieve freedom and equality, and not allow a part of the entire Chinese nation to be assimilated outside the territory. Over the years, there have been some achievements, and people in society have often praised it. Now the university has reached the beginning of the fourth academic year, with more than twenty departments in five colleges, and the scale is roughly complete. The middle school has also been reorganized and is improving day by day. However, the school is still in the process of improvement. Recalling the past three years, I was trapped in economic storms and constant winds and rains. In addition, Jinan is in a special situation, because the middle school and the single-subject university were reorganized by Hongnian into a complete university, which is completely different from the schools that have been established and have rules to follow. Various constructions require funds everywhere. Special equipment has only received warehouse receipts for 300,000 yuan, and the actual cash is only more than 250,000 yuan. Other schools receive the same treatment, and it is not only Jinan that is favored. At the beginning of Hongnian's tenure, he first cleared old debts and reissued arrears, totaling 70,000 yuan. In the seventeenth year, the grade levels were added according to the regulations. From July, expenses were made according to the new budget, but the income remained the same. In addition, the discount was issued, and the subsidy from the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office was stopped. With this increase and decrease, there was a shortfall of 20,000 yuan per month for seven months. Until March of last year, it was possible to receive the new budget. The operation and planning in this were all done by Hongnian in various ways, using his own thin property to mortgage to the bank. He successively added more than ten buildings, including the Science Museum Auditorium, offices, faculty and staff dormitories, and male and female student dormitories, and added school equipment and increased books and instruments. The cost was not insignificant. The old appearance of the school has changed, and the new debts of individuals have been heavily burdened. The debts have reached more than ten million yuan. Hongnian only thought it was for the sake of the school, endured the pain and worked hard to support it. Why is it so old? It is nothing more than recalling the merits of the overseas Chinese in assisting the revolution, feeling the Party-state's entrustment to educate the household, and striving to complete the highest institution of overseas Chinese, to reward the Premier for the overseas Chinese's assistance in the revolution, to comfort the spirit in heaven, and to fulfill the responsibility of a healthy party member, regardless of the pros and cons. Therefore, although he once went to assist in financial management and twice assisted in industry and commerce, it was not necessary. After entering the ministry, he did not spend the 200 yuan per month that he only received from the school. However, he never regarded the school as a side business. Therefore, when he lived in Beijing, the school affairs were always full of letters and telegrams. There were many express packages every day, and there were vouchers to check. The receiving and sending books can also be checked. He also worried that the handling may be negligent. Every Monday and Saturday, he left Beijing for Shanghai to personally handle school administration, discuss school affairs with teachers and staff, always for six or seven hours every day, and attended the memorial week, reporting on the points of improvement at any time. In the past three years, except for attending the Premier's funeral and summer vacation or special events, he has not missed a week to attend the memorial, giving deep instructions to the students. The school publication can be checked. In this way, running between Beijing and Shanghai, traveling in the dust, with his heart hanging in two places, Hongnian's remaining life of worries, whether in politics or education, can be said to be over. He only remembers that he has received special knowledge from the Premier in the past, and is ashamed of not having an inch of repayment. He has cultivated the field of overseas Chinese education, and he cannot continue to cultivate it. Fortunately, the government has decided that university presidents cannot hold concurrent positions. Hongnian, in his foolishness, also deeply believes that education is the fundamental plan of the country, and overseas Chinese education has a special mission. Rejoicing in the opportunity, he humbly wishes to get rid of his official career and devote himself to education. Moreover, he has a historical relationship with Jinan. Once the school base is consolidated and the construction is completed, he will cleanly retreat. He can comfort the Premier and feel at ease in his conscience. He humbly hopes that you will be considerate of his foolishness and immediately submit a proposal to the council to exempt him from his position as Political Deputy of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, so that he can devote himself wholeheartedly to overseas Chinese education, so as to be effective. I am sincerely grateful for your friendship. Sincerely presenting to the Executive Yuan, Zheng Hongnian, President of National Jinan University.

Flexibility in the Deadline for Registration of Primary Schools:

The Ministry of Education, according to a report from the Zhejiang Education Department, issued an instruction from your ministry to clearly define the deadline for registration of private schools at all levels in various places, and ordered them to follow the instructions and report. Upon investigation, private secondary schools in Zhejiang Province that have not been registered have been ordered to complete the registration procedures within the first semester of the 19th year. If the same strict order is issued to private primary schools in various places to register within the deadline, there will be many obstacles in practice. For example, most of the private primary schools in various places are established by rural people or the groups they organize. The villagers are not clear about the laws and regulations. If the deadline is strictly set and registration is urged, it is easy to arouse resentment, reduce the enthusiasm for running schools, or even close down. This is one. According to the current situation, primary school education is far from popular. For private schools, the main thing is to encourage improvement. For private primary schools, it is difficult to use the same strict rules. This is two. Furthermore, the number of primary schools run by local churches is still large, and it takes a lot of time to negotiate restrictions. This is three. In summary, it seems that the deadline for registration of private schools should be handled separately for primary and secondary schools. It is appropriate to prepare a document for reporting, and to request your approval for compliance. The Ministry of Education instructed, "The report is known. The deadline for registration of private schools can be specified separately for primary and secondary schools. Private secondary schools in the province that have not been registered have been ordered by the department to complete the registration procedures within the first semester of the 19th year, and should be handled within the deadline. As for the private primary schools in the province that have not been registered, the department has found that there are difficulties, and all registration deadlines can be appropriately extended. Please follow the instructions."

Public School Graduation Certificates Can Be Stamped by City and County Education Bureaus

The Ministry of Education, based on a request from the Fujian Provincial Department of Education regarding whether graduation certificates from public schools can be stamped by city and county education bureaus, instructed that graduation certificates from public schools should be approved to follow the regulations for school graduation and completion certificates, specifically Article 4, Section 3, and be stamped by the city or county education bureau where the school is located. This is to be noted and implemented accordingly.

Ministry of Education Explains Qualifications of Normal School Graduates

Chen Baohe, a graduate of the Ba County Normal School, inquired with the Ministry of Education about the equivalent qualifications of a two-year graduate of a public normal school under the old system compared to schools under the new system, and whether they can directly apply to specialized schools. The Ministry of Education replied that, upon review, the regulations for old-system normal schools varied. If the student graduated from a higher primary school before entering the normal school, then two years of study there would be equivalent to completing the second year of junior high school. As for qualifications for entering specialized schools, the regulations clearly state that applicants must have graduated from a public or officially registered private senior high school or an equivalent institution, and must pass the entrance examination. Even the preparatory courses require graduates from old-system middle schools according to the above regulations, this student cannot directly apply to a specialized school.

Anhui Province Restricts Transfer Policies for Government-Funded Students

The Anhui Provincial Department of Education recently established measures to restrict government-funded students from transferring schools and has already sent notices to embassies and student supervisors abroad to inform Anhui students. The measures are as follows: 1. Students studying abroad must complete three years of coursework at their original institution and achieve excellent grades with a corresponding degree before applying for a transfer. 2. Students transferring to another country will continue to receive the original stipend, with the total duration, including the time spent in the original country, not exceeding six years. 3. Government-funded students returning to China will receive travel expenses according to the original country of study's regulations.

Jiangsu Provincial Education College Holds Autumn Cocoon Exhibition in the People's Education Experiment Zone

The Jiangsu Provincial Education College's People's Education Experiment Zone has been in operation for a year and a half, with every effort made to develop various undertakings in the zone. Recently, recognizing that sericulture is the main sideline for nearby residents, the zone, in order to improve people's lives and revitalize the local silk industry, has specially invited sericulture expert Mr. Miao Zhen to provide sericulture guidance starting this year. He is encouraging families to try raising autumn silkworms, using improved silkworm breeds and new sericulture methods. The general public, seeing the potential benefits, are all happy to comply. The silkworm breeds used are from the Huxuguan Renxu Hall and the Luoshe Great China. The Experiment Zone disinfects all silkworm rearing rooms and equipment for the silkworm farmers. Simultaneously, the Experiment Zone is raising demonstration silkworms to serve as a model for the people, and providing guidance to each household twice daily, morning and afternoon. The silkworm farmers readily accept the instructions of the instructors, and therefore, the autumn cocoon harvest of the guided silkworm farmers this year is particularly abundant, the quality has improved, and the selling price is also high, making everyone happy. It is reported that the zone, in order to encourage silkworm farmers to adopt improved silkworm breeds and improved rearing methods, has specifically scheduled an autumn cocoon exhibition at the Experiment Zone's auditorium for two days starting on the 30th of this month. The cocoons of each silkworm farmer will be assessed and ranked, and displayed accordingly. In addition, various models, specimens, and posters related to sericulture will also be displayed. The zone is currently working on preparations, dividing into groups to proceed. On the evening of October 1st, an awards ceremony and various recreational activities will also be held.

A New Contribution to Rural Economic Research

Professor Buck of Jinling University authored a book on Chinese agricultural economics. Scholars who have studied rural economics in recent years often lament the lack of relevant materials for reference. The Department of Agricultural Economics of the College of Agriculture at Jinling University, seeking to remedy this deficiency, has diligently and assiduously collected and organized such materials for over a decade. For example, Mr. Qiao Qiming's work on population issues and the tenant farming system, Mr. Sun Wenyu's work on food issues, and Mr. Xu Cheng's work on rural cooperation have all been continuous and excellent contributions, and have been highly regarded by scholars. Recently, Professor Buck of the department has published a new work, the content of which is based on the results of a comprehensive survey of 2,866 farm households in 17 locations across seven provinces from 1921 to 1925. It provides highly detailed statistics on land use, farm size, land ownership, the tenant farming system, farm labor, rural population, food consumption, and living standards. The original work is in English, titled "Chinese Farm Economy," and is 500 pages long with numerous charts and tables. All theories are based on numerical data, eliminating the shortcomings of empty and abstract discussions. It is truly an unprecedented masterpiece in the field of rural economics in our country. The exclusive domestic distributor is the Shanghai Commercial Press. The translation is being undertaken by Mr. Qiao Qiming and Mr. Zhang Luluan from the department, and it is reported that the majority has been completed and will be published soon.

Shanghai Experimental Elementary School Problem Experiment Report

The Shanghai Middle School Experimental Elementary School, located on Shangwen Road in this city, pays close attention to experimental work and actively promotes small-problem experiments. Several experiments have been completed and published, such as the comparative experimental report on the arrangement method of fractional teaching materials, the comparative experimental report on the teaching method of arithmetic principles, the comparative experimental report on the problem of reciting short vernacular essays, the comparative experimental report on the writing teaching stroke order problem, and the comparative experimental report on the composition correction problem. Now, the first report on small-problem experiments has been published, with the content divided into theoretical and practical parts, titled "The Theory and Practice of Small-Problem Experiments." The description is quite detailed and helpful to the elementary education community. It is reported that this publication is not for sale, and colleagues in education can request a copy by attaching five cents in postage. In addition, the school's new research and tutoring series, 20 publications in total, have also been published successively, with affordable prices. The comprehensive report for the past three years will also be published soon.

Local News

Salt Revenue Loans Still Able to Pay Interest on Schedule

Minister Song's Speech Yesterday

Finance Minister Song Ziwen made the following statement to the National News Agency regarding the repayment of salt revenue loans:

It has been a year since I issued a statement regarding salt revenue loans on September 18th of last year. Although the situation has been unstable and exchange rates have soared, the government has raised the necessary funds and paid all items due under the original salt revenue loans before September 30th of this year on schedule. The aforementioned debts due include two types of interest coupons due on April 5th and October 5th of this year for the British-French loan, the June interest coupon for the Hukwang loan (estimated at 140,000 pounds, which exceeds the 950,000 taels of silver strongly allocated to the salt tax under the customs), and three periods of interest coupons due on April 1st, October 1st of the 18th year, and April 1st of the 19th year for the Crisp loan. In September of the 18th year, the government paid two types of interest coupons for the British-French loan, thereby clearing all outstanding interest on these loans. As for the interest coupon due on October 1st of the 19th year for the Crisp loan, it has been scheduled for payment at the end of this year. Therefore, the interest owed on the above two loans in the 16th and 17th years can be fully cleared by the end of this year. After clearing the outstanding interest, the government will devote itself to repaying the outstanding principal in order to clear them in turn. The details of this method are described in the statement issued on September 18th of the 18th year. As for the interest payment due on July 1st of the 19th year for the Crisp loan, because Yan Xishan seized a large amount of salt tax in his jurisdiction and delayed remitting it to the central government, the government was unable to repay it on schedule. At the time, it was felt that a solution might be found by temporarily delaying the July interest payment on one hand and actively urging Yan to hand over the funds on the other. Now, the funds have indeed been remitted to the central government a few days ago. The administration of salt tax has been reorganized and improved by the Salt Revenue Audit Office over the past year, with much progress. The situation has been so unstable, but the salt revenue loans are still able to pay interest on schedule, which is what the Ministry is comforted by.
