Fandiwen's Talk

Yesterday Morning's Reception for Chinese and Foreign Journalists

Former Belgian Foreign Minister Mr. Paul Hymans yesterday met with Chinese and foreign journalists at the Foreign Affairs Discussion Committee on Avenue Joffre, giving a public talk for about an hour and a half. The following is a record of the meeting:

Mission to China

Mr. Hymans first answered reporters about the purpose of his trip, saying that he was invited by the Academia Sinica as a university professor to come to China to study social movements, political conditions, and so on. His purpose was to learn. He had to clearly state that this trip had absolutely nothing to do with politics. Moreover, his time in China was still short, and his observations were very incomplete. Therefore, he was not yet able to express concrete opinions about his impressions of China. When he was in the North, he was able to contact political figures. Regarding the labor movement, apart from seeing books on the Chinese labor movement in Europe, he has not actually had contact with Chinese workers. He currently has no research or study period on the Chinese labor movement. However, in Beiping, he spent a lot of time studying Chinese art and deeply felt that China's artistic civilization was worthy of great admiration. After arriving in Shanghai, he spoke with friends yesterday and felt that during the revolutionary process in China, although internal wars rose and fell continuously, China's social, economic, and educational undertakings were still progressing, which was also worthy of great admiration. As for Chinese politics, he was unwilling to express opinions, not because the Chinese revolution had not yet succeeded. Cromwell's revolution in England took 200 years to complete, and the French Revolution of 1798 also took 100 years to build a democratic government. The Chinese revolution has been going on for less than 20 years. He saw communist slogans yesterday calling him a running dog of imperialism, which was truly unjust. When he was the Belgian Foreign Minister, he expressed great sympathy for China. He played a role in the return of the Belgian concession in Tianjin to China. When he was Foreign Minister, he was vigorously attacked by the Belgian conservatives. Now that he is in Shanghai, he plans to give several public lectures. The topics and lectures have not yet been determined. He gave lectures in the North on: (1) A comparison between the Second International and the First International; (2) A comparison between the Three Principles of the People and Socialism; (3) The organization of international peace and its guarantee. It is also possible that he will repeat these three topics in Shanghai. Regarding his lectures, although he is the leader of the Second International and the Belgian Socialist Party, his purpose is to conduct theoretical analysis, not to promote doctrines.

European Peace

Mr. Hymans next answered about the future of European peace, saying that the discord between France and Italy was seen by many as a cause for concern about the outbreak of a second world war. He encountered the same question when he was in Japan. However, he firmly believed that there was absolutely no danger of a second world war breaking out in Europe in the near future. When he was at the League of Nations in Geneva, he talked about this matter with Czech President Tomáš Masaryk. The Czech President used an analogy, saying that fire cannot burn without fuel. His meaning was that in 1914, Europe was full of fuel, which caused the great fire of the European War. Now that the fuel has been burned to ashes, there is nothing left to burn, so how can a fire start? That is one reason. Now, without discussing the governments of European countries, but speaking of the people of Europe, it can be said that no one does not hate war. Moreover, the military strength of the nations is evenly matched. If they want to start a war, they must first win over and organize alliances to break the balance of power. However, this is impossible in the near future. Therefore, although the authorities of some countries occasionally make dangerous remarks, they are just bluffing and do not actually dare to risk the world's condemnation by starting a war with no certainty of success. French Foreign Minister Aristide Briand once declared that as long as he is in office, he will never allow war to happen. That is the second reason. Furthermore, there are now two major forces in Europe, democratic politics and dictatorial politics, competing with each other. If the forces of democracy gain an advantage in the future, there will be no danger to European peace. Conversely, if the forces of dictatorship gain an advantage, then the future of European peace cannot be easily predicted. However, he is confident that the current dictatorial politics are a reaction to the European War, and the future of Europe will inevitably be the world of democratic politics. It can be predicted. Perhaps the victory of the far-right National Socialist Party in the German elections will cause problems for the overall situation in Europe. He believes that this is also a temporary phenomenon. Moreover, the National Socialist Party once held a dominant position in the German parliament in 1924, but no major changes occurred at that time. However, if the German National Socialist Party rises to form a government, there may be some implications.

German-French Relations

Mr. Hymans was asked about Germany's attitude toward the Treaty of Versailles, whether it would demand revision, cancellation, or fulfillment. He replied that most people in Germany hope to revise the Treaty of Versailles through political and diplomatic means in a friendly manner, and have no intention of resorting to force. The German representative made this statement at the Locarno Conference in 1925. As for the Western European border issues stipulated in the Treaty of Versailles, such as the return of Alsace-Lorraine to France and the recognition of Belgium's complete independence, the Locarno Treaty confirmed these two points. Germany also recognizes these two points as established facts with no room for revision. Because the Treaty of Versailles had the drawbacks of the victorious countries forcibly presiding over the defeated countries, the Locarno Treaty was negotiated by the German representative based on the diplomatic policies of former German Foreign Minister Gustav Stresemann, with free will and without objection.

League of Nations

Finally, Mr. Hymans spoke about the League of Nations and Briand's European Union plan, saying that the League of Nations takes the attitude of the participating countries' governments as its attitude. If the representatives of the participating countries belong to the Conservative Party, it is difficult to expect them to seek benefits for small and weak nations. If they are progressives, they are more likely to take care of the welfare of small and weak nations. As for Briand's European Union plan, all countries have expressed agreement in principle. However, due to the different nature of each country's government, they each have several reservations about the European Union plan. He acknowledges that this plan is ideal, but fears that it will be difficult to become a reality. As for the saying that there is a Fourth International organization in Europe, he has never heard of it. It may be an organization of the Italian Socialist Party contacting socialist parties in other countries.

Grand Banquet at the Tahua Hotel Last Night

Last night, representatives from various organizations held a public banquet at the Tahua Hotel. In addition to Mr. Hymans, those present included Central Committee members Li Shizeng and Cai Yuanpei, former envoy to Belgium Wang Jingqi, Zheng Yuxiu, Chen Shiguang, Liu Yunfang, and more than a hundred representatives from various organizations. It was a very grand banquet celebrating Sino-Belgian friendship. Mr. Cai Yuanpei presided over the meeting and delivered a welcoming speech, saying, "Today, the Academia Sinica, together with various organizations in Shanghai, welcome Mr. Paul Hymans and his wife. We are deeply honored by the presence of Mr. and Mrs. Hymans. Modern sociological theories, since the era of economic revolution, have gradually studied, improved, or manufactured natural materials to serve the world in the second half of the 19th century. As a result, industry has developed rapidly. If we want industrial development, we must unite labor and capital. In theory, both labor and capital should help each other and harmonize to seek the happiness of all mankind. However, the reality is often not the case. Sometimes there are minor conflicts between the two sides that can be resolved immediately. Sometimes the problems are complex and even lead to disputes, leading to bloodshed and war. Therefore, sociologists have devised ways to improve the treatment of workers, either by enacting laws or by forming organizations. Recently, there has been an organization of international labor groups to seek the happiness of workers around the world. The number of workers who benefit from this fact is in the tens of thousands. The completeness of its organization and the magnitude of its responsibility can be imagined. All of this is planned by a small number of sociologists, and Mr. Hymans is one of the most effective and important members. China's social situation is slightly different from that of other countries. China is currently in a political revolution, similar to Europe in the 1830s. At that time, all the states of Europe underwent major political reforms. After a few years, they gradually became stable and entered the era of economic revolution. The economic revolution occurred, and the problem of capital and labor arose, leading to various complex and unfortunate events. Labor-capital disputes in Europe will inevitably occur in China in the future. After the political revolution in China, an economic revolution will inevitably occur. Once there is an economic revolution, there will inevitably be the same complex social problems. All of these cannot be resolved at present. At present, general economic panic has spread to all countries in the world, and the number of unemployed people has increased rapidly. According to statistics, there are 2 million unemployed people in the United Kingdom, 4 million in the United States, 3 million in Germany, and 400,000 in Japan. The actual causes are nothing more than the following two points: (1) Overproduction: there are more manufactured goods than buyers; (2) Each country has its own self-defense tariff law. The purpose of the self-defense tariff law is nothing more than to reduce imports from other countries, but the exports of the country do not increase. The number of unemployed people therefore increases accordingly. Regarding the second cause, Mr. Hymans advocates using international reciprocal tariffs to alleviate the situation. As for the first cause, each country must find its own solution, but the best method has not yet been discovered today. From the above-mentioned various problems, it can be seen that the social movement of a country changes with the economic situation. Before China reaches the era of economic revolution, how should we study the various labor-capital disputes that have occurred in Europe over the past few decades and the current situation to learn from? Now that we have the guidance of Mr. Hymans, we may hope to solve China's future labor-capital problems in advance. This is what my colleagues and I deeply hope for. I hereby represent the various organizations in China to express our sincere welcome and raise our glasses to wish you good health."

Opening of the 7th National Anti-Drug Week

Today is the National Day of Shame for Anti-Drug Use

Delegate Assembly to be Held this Afternoon

The long-planned 7th National Anti-Drug Week has been jointly prepared by party and government organs at all levels, groups, anti-drug branches, and anti-drug propaganda associations in provinces, cities, and counties across the country and will begin today. In Shanghai, all parties have enthusiastically joined the preparations. The following is a summary of the anti-drug week, which has attracted attention both at home and abroad and has become popular throughout the country:

The purpose of this session: The scourge of opium and all narcotic drugs is the main cause and result of China's failed diplomacy and frequent internal strife, weakening the national structure, creating social chaos, withering party businesses, and impoverishing people's lives. The association witnessed great difficulties and initiated anti-drug efforts to eradicate domestic opium and stop foreign drugs. Since 1924, a National Anti-Drug Week has been held every autumn to awaken compatriots to rise up against drugs. Since its implementation, it has lasted for six sessions, and the news has spread and aroused the whole country. This year marks the seventh session. Looking around at the darkness of the environment, we feel the greater the responsibility and the greater the hope. We deeply hope that compatriots across the country will swear with the utmost sincerity, make persistent efforts, and complete the anti-drug campaign to eliminate all drug scourges. The future of the party and the country depends on this. Please, compatriots, encourage each other.

Preparation process: For this Anti-Drug Week, the Anti-Drug Association of the Republic of China sent letters to party and government organs at all levels throughout the country and overseas Chinese communities, asking them to jointly prepare with anti-drug groups in advance. Those preparing to hold activities this time include more than 400 cities and counties in the provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, Guangdong, Jiangxi, Yunnan, Henan, and Shandong. Overseas areas such as Singapore in Southeast Asia are also preparing to hold activities.

Measures for the Day of Shame: Today is the first day of Anti-Drug Week. The meaning, purpose, and measures announced on this day are as follows: (A) Meaning: Opium is the main cause of unequal treaties. For more than 80 years, China's diplomacy has failed, its internal affairs have not been rectified, bandits have been rampant, and traitors have been rampant, all due to the scourge of opium. How can we not express a deep sense of shame and humiliation for this great humiliation that has caused great pain, so as to awaken the public to fight together? Therefore, there is a Day of Shame for the Anti-Drug Week to awaken compatriots to wash away this great humiliation. (B) Purpose: As the saying goes, knowing shame is akin to courage. The movement of the Day of Shame for Anti-Drug Use is intended to make the general public have a deep understanding and thorough awareness of the opium aggression conspiracy and various policies of the imperialists, and to have the determination to eliminate it and move forward courageously to achieve the purpose of shame. (C) Measures: 1. Party organs, groups, schools, at all levels shall hold anti-drug lectures, recite Sun Yat-sen's anti-drug testament, lecture on the history of opium's harm to the country, and the anti-drug mission of the people. 2. Newspapers and magazines shall issue special publications and carry more news about anti-drug use and the significance of this session, so as to awaken the public. 3. Local public anti-drug groups shall carry out anti-drug propaganda and send personnel to various districts to give lectures. 4. Groups shall hold oath-taking campaigns and actively promote anti-drug monthly publications and various anti-drug publications. (D) Outline of propaganda for the Day of Shame: Today, China suffers from the scourge of opium, which has led to rampant bandits, repeated famines, withered industries, and impoverished people's lives. To trace the source and investigate the root cause, there is no one who does not recall the history of opium's entry into China. The entry of opium into China began with the Opium War between China and Britain in the late Qing Dynasty. First, the British seized the trade privileges of the Portuguese in East Asia, and then transported opium produced in their territory of India to China in large quantities to harm the bodies of our people and absorb the money of our people. By 1836, the British had smuggled more than 20,000 boxes of opium into China, worth as much as 17,904,248 taels of silver. In 1839, Lin Zexu ordered the prohibition of opium in Guangdong and burned tens of thousands of boxes of British opium. As a result, conflicts broke out with the British. The British government then sent a large army to attack the seaports of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, and Zhili. Our army was defeated, and as a result, the British were compensated with more than 20 million taels of silver for the value of opium and military expenses, which led to the beginning of unequal treaties. From then on, the British did their best to poison the Chinese people. Since then, the people have become poor and the country has become weak, and the situation has deteriorated. Other countries have followed suit and used various unequal treaties to implement their policy of letting the scourge of drugs run rampant. China is under the power of the great powers and can only be slaughtered and bullied. In recent years, the import of morphine, heroin, cocaine, etc., which are far more harmful than opium, has increased even more. The annual import from foreign countries reaches more than 80 million taels, and the financial loss has been tens of millions of yuan, and the harm suffered by the people is even more difficult to estimate. In addition, foreigners have set up factories in China to manufacture morphine and sell it to our country.

Page 14

All over the country. In addition, concessions are the center of opium trade and the general base of drug indulgence. Overseas Chinese living in various colonies are subjected to the opium scourge of the local colonial governments. The evidence is clear and cannot be concealed. They are implementing their opium monopoly policy to increase income, raise the army and navy, and consolidate their position, at the expense of the interests of millions of overseas Chinese. Their perverse acts are outrageous. In order to prevent the attack of fair world opinion, they declare in various countries that Chinese people's addiction to opium has become a natural nature, thereby deceiving the world and concealing their ugliness. For example, the International Opium Conference is postponed indefinitely to avoid our country's questioning, and an unfair Far East Investigation Group is organized specifically to expose our country's shortcomings. All of this is heartbreaking to say. Today's anti-drug campaign is an important plan to save the country and strengthen the race. At this time when foreign aggression is rampant and the scourge of drugs is rampant, we should pay attention to the following points: (1) Strive to abolish unequal treaties. The various facts of losing power and humiliating the country that China has suffered for a hundred years are marked by the scourge of opium. Therefore, if we want to seek fundamental remedies, we must strive to abolish unequal treaties. The import of opium and drugs is entirely supported by unequal treaties, which are used to promote its conspiracy to poison China. Today, we are advocating the anti-drug campaign in order to gather the strength of compatriots across the country to attack this unbreakable unequal treaty and strive to achieve the goal of silencing it. (2) Secondly, strive to realize the proposal to limit the manufacture of drugs in the world to the extent necessary for scientific use. The great powers regard our country as a drug market, and the whole world knows it. Today, the reason why our country's livelihood is bankrupt and its national power is in danger is actually given by the great powers. We have already reached the point of being unbearable to watch. Unexpectedly, in recent years, in addition to exporting opium to China as much as possible, various countries have even manufactured drugs in large quantities, such as morphine and heroin, and tried every means to transport them to China to poison our country. There is nothing more inhuman and unreasonable than this. After the launch of China's anti-drug campaign, we advocated a proposal to limit the manufacture of drugs and made appeals to the international community in an effort to achieve an early conclusion. However, the speakers were earnest and the listeners were contemptuous. Not only have the drug manufacturing plants in various countries not decreased, but they have also been increasing day by day, and the harm our country has suffered has also been increasing. This is what my colleagues and I are deeply concerned about. The most urgent plan at present is to resolutely revitalize ourselves, strictly and vigorously eliminate the planting, transportation, sale, and smoking of opium in the country to stop the mouths of foreigners, and then expose the truth of the great powers' scourge of China, so that they have nowhere to hide, in order to seek international justice. (3) Overseas Chinese are suffering from the scourge of opium. Colonial governments use this as an important source of tax revenue and disregard the lives of hundreds of thousands of overseas Chinese. At this critical moment, if we do not quickly seek remedies, we will not stop until the race is destroyed and the country is destroyed. Overseas Chinese have now launched an anti-drug campaign, and there are already many who are engaged in organizing. This phenomenon is enough to promote the early death of the great powers' opium policy. I sincerely hope that overseas compatriots will unite and thoroughly strive for the anti-drug campaign to complete the scourge of drugs that has not stopped for a hundred years, and the country's economy and people's livelihood will benefit immensely.

Opening Ceremony: Today at 2:00 pm, the opening ceremony will be held at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. Various groups and organs in the city, as well as enthusiastic comrades, have been invited to participate. Invitations have already been sent out, and celebrities have been invited to give speeches. The opening declaration is specially recorded as follows: Today is the opening day of the 7th National Anti-Drug Week. Looking back on our past struggles and looking at the current situation of the spread of the scourge of tobacco, what kind of feelings will arise? Today, there is a shortage of food and high rice prices, which have not been seen for decades. In the northwest provinces, famine is imminent, and starving people are everywhere. The tragic situation of the people cannot be described in words. There are many reasons for this. Opium is actually the cause of all this. The warlords in the Northwest not only forced farmers to plant tobacco in order to collect heavy taxes, but also forced the chambers of commerce to buy soil in order to facilitate sales. The tobacco seedlings in Sichuan, Guizhou, Yunnan, and Guangxi are all over the place. Farmers refuse drugs and are fined for neglecting donations. This is an unprecedented event, seen under the blue sky and white sun. In the provinces of Fujian and Anhui, they are secretly transported to the capital. Beside the ban, tobacco flowers are in full bloom. What is more contradictory than this? The authorities in Wuhan sell opium and collect special taxes. According to reliable statistics, there are only 536 rice shops in the city, but there are as many as 764 soil shops. Ships come and go, openly transporting goods, and the prohibition law is swept away. In the North China area, heroin is prevalent, and smokers die in two or three years. The authorities are busy with political infighting and have not even taken care of it. Even the army is addicted, accounting for the majority. Shanghai is the general base of opium. Major cases have been cracked repeatedly, but none have been investigated. Now there are even red pills, which are hundreds of times more poisonous than opium, all over the place. As for foreign anesthetic drug factories, there are more and more of them, and the number has reached more than 130. The main market is our country. Of the 20 million taels of Persian opium that were exported last year, 80 to 90 percent entered our country. Overseas Chinese in the Nanyang Islands are addicted to opium, and the colonial government encourages them to collect huge taxes, regardless of the lives of hundreds of thousands of overseas Chinese. The opium used annually is actually more than 19 million taels.

China, a country with poor people and exhausted resources, can no longer bear this scourge of internal and external aggression. If this harm is not eliminated, the chaos of politics, the violence of soldiers, the withering of industry, and the impoverishment of people's livelihood will all deteriorate and be beyond repair. We cannot bear to see the people committing suicide, so we must quickly catch up and seek a way to eliminate this harm. We have not been able to overthrow the evil forces behind opium. We should do our best to automatically refuse drugs, first remove our bad habits, clear the harm of drugs in the family, and use the power of the group to clean up the bad habits in society, swear to reject drugs, and never compromise. If we can do this, the demand for opium will decrease, and those who plant, transport, sell, and smoke opium will inevitably change to other jobs. There are government offices that force people to plant tobacco, but there are no government offices that force people to smoke. The fundamental solution is still in ourselves. As the saying goes, people insult themselves, then others insult them. If a country must attack itself, then others will attack it. The scourge of opium is also the same. Therefore, under these circumstances, we should have a fresh awakening. Do not entrust the responsibility of banning opium entirely to government offices. Everyone should make up their minds, and every family should be like this. Recognize that refusing drugs is the right way to wash away national shame, and abiding by the law is a necessary condition for banning opium. When the family is united, we should first remove the bad habit of smoking, strengthen our physique, and never give up smoking. Other measures, such as eliminating tobacco seedlings to stop famine, and stopping anesthetic drugs to protect the health of the race, can then be used to plan construction and make the country rich and strong. This is the significance of this session and the principle of our struggle. The Anti-Drug Association of the Republic of China has gathered anti-drug comrades from all over the country and has fought against the dark forces many times, but the results have not been obvious and the scourge of tobacco is still rampant. This is because the association's responsibility has not been fulfilled and the society's support has not been exhausted. We hope that people across the country will cooperate and not just talk empty words, but do practical things. This is the only condition for the success of anti-drug use and the unavoidable journey of banning opium. We respectfully offer this to the people of the country.

Today's Phenomena in This City: Great slogans on Nanjing Road: Starting today, extremely large cloth slogans in Chinese and English will be hung between the Sincere and Wing On companies on Nanjing Road in order to make people shocked. The Shanghai Municipal Council has approved the matter, and the transportation agencies are cooperating. The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Party Departments are responsible for posting anti-drug week color picture slogans at more than 90 stations on the two railways. The public buses and trams in the Chinese areas of Zhabei and Nanshi, and the public buses in the public concession, are all posting various anti-drug propaganda materials. Aircraft distribute leaflets: The Naval Headquarters has been consulted to send multiple aircraft to distribute leaflets. Theaters show anti-drug slides: The Anti-Drug Association believes that improving customs, exposing people's hearts, and film propaganda are most effective. The association has specially consulted theaters in this city to show anti-drug slides before each film screening during the anti-drug week. Celebrity speeches: Tonight, Comrade Yang Qingyuan, Minister of the Propaganda Department of the Municipal Party Committee, will broadcast a speech.

Sharp Decline in Cotton Production in Various Districts

Farmers' Economy Feels Even More Difficult

For the past half month, autumn rains and autumn winds have been continuous. It is the time when cotton crops are blooming and budding. Due to the damage caused by the wind and rain, countless flowers and buds have fallen off, and cotton bolls have rotted and fallen to the ground in various districts of the city. The quality is poor, the output has declined sharply, and the farmers' economy has suffered huge losses. The cotton farmers are all worried. This year, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau has conducted cooperative cotton planting experiments in the districts of Lixing, Zhenru, Caojing, Pusong, and Yangsi, totaling 39 locations. Some of them have also been affected equally. At present, the cotton crops in various districts have been harvested. The highest yield is about 100 catties, and the lowest is only 20 to 30 catties.

Agricultural and Mining Ministry Agricultural Product Improvement Discussion Committee

Established Yesterday

For the purpose of studying and improving various agricultural products in our country, the Ministry of Agriculture and Mines has specially appointed Ye Huijun, Gu Xinyi, Wang Yaochen, Wang Xiaolai, Cai Jiansan, Rong Zongjing, Sun Jingxi, Lu Wenshao, Zheng Chengqing, etc., as well as other agricultural experts, as members of the Agricultural Product Improvement Discussion Committee, and designated Xu Tinghu, Director of the Agricultural Administration Department, Jin Wensi, Director and Deputy Directors Cai Wuji, Yu Qianshan, and Jiang Hanlu, etc., of the Shanghai Agricultural Products Inspection Institute, to also serve as members of the committee. Yesterday, the Ministry of Agriculture and Mines specially sent Director Jin and Deputy Director Cai as representatives of Minister Yi to host a banquet for the committee members. Except for Cai Jiansan, who did not attend, and Rong Zongjing, who was represented by Wang Yaochen, all others attended the meeting. Director Jin immediately reported on the purpose of the committee, stating that China is founded on agriculture, and improving agricultural products is related to the foundation of the country, a matter of great importance. The Ministry of Agriculture still needs to select and appoint agricultural experts from across the country to discuss together. Therefore, today's banquet is a preliminary reception to exchange ideas, and a formal conference will be held later. He invited everyone to attend, express their great opinions, and contribute to the government. The committee members successively expressed their opinions, and the meeting ended in a joyful atmosphere.

County First District Office Reports on Disaster and Famine

Due to various natural disasters in the past, the first district of the county has suffered a famine. Now, the document submitted by the district office to the county government is recorded as follows: Due to frequent natural disasters and poor cotton harvest, it is reported that personnel should be sent to conduct on-site inspections. According to the report from Jiang Yuanbu and others, the head of Qinxiang Township, stating that since the beginning of summer this year, fortunately the weather has been warm and the rainfall has been even, various crops have been able to be planted in time. Unexpectedly, on the afternoon of July 3rd, hail fell from the sky, destroying all the cotton seedlings, forming an unprecedented and strange disaster. The officials immediately reported it to your department and forwarded it to the county government, which sent personnel to conduct on-site inspections and confirmed the situation. At the same time, the officials advised and persuaded the farmers to endure the pain and purchase seeds for replanting in order to seek relief. However, when the villagers were replanting, it was already past the planting season, and the development was not as neat and vigorous as before. However, if water and drought were timely and no accidents occurred, then even if the initial loss was significant, it might still be possible to make up for it later. Unexpectedly, from Minor Heat to Major Heat, separated by forty or fifty days, when the cotton flowers and bolls were forming and needed moisture and nutrients urgently, the weather did not rain and suffered a second strike. During this period, the disaster situation was already obvious. However, when the cotton was about to bloom, fortunately, there was a heavy rain, although it was late, there was still hope for a medium harvest year. Unfortunately, heaven did not follow man's wishes, and the continuous rain lasted for ten days, causing the cotton stalks to be steamed by the moisture, and the branches and leaves grew more luxuriantly, while the cotton bolls rotted and fell off one after another. As a result, the harvest suffered a major loss. Now, although it is harvest time, the yield per acre is only about two or three tenths of the normal yield. In the future, the entire harvest will only be about three or four tenths in quality. Considering that rice prices have soared this year and all goods are expensive, and planting in time has already cost a lot, and after the hail damage, replanting has been costly. Now, with no hope of harvest this autumn, what will the small people do for the winter? Therefore, they jointly reported to the district head, hoping that you would consider the difficulties of the people and quickly forward the report to the county government to send personnel to conduct on-site inspections, reduce and postpone taxes, and at the same time find ways to provide relief to alleviate the people's suffering. Based on this, it is believed that the hail this year is a major cause of the disaster and famine. Previously, it was reported to your government to send personnel to investigate and clarify the situation. Later, the weather became flooded or drought, which is also the most important component of the disaster. According to the reports from the heads of various townships, the harvest is only three or four tenths, which is indeed the actual situation. Considering that rice prices have soared this year, exceeding 20 yuan per stone, the villagers have replanted again and again, exhausting their resources, increasing unexpected labor costs, and suffering this ruthless disaster, the people's livelihood is deeply sympathized. In addition to approving the forwarding of the report to your government and jointly planning relief measures with the heads of various townships, the situation of the disaster is reported accordingly, requesting that your government quickly send personnel to the district to conduct on-site inspections, determine the composition of the disaster, and submit a report at each level to request reduction and postponement of taxes, and at the same time find ways to provide relief to alleviate the people's suffering, which is truly in the public interest.

Agricultural Inspection Institute Approves Registration of Wheat Inventory

Separate Temporary Registration Measures for Inventory

The Shanghai Agricultural Products Inspection Institute has set October 1st as the start date for inspecting and examining wheat transported and sold in Shanghai in order to eliminate malpractices such as mixing with cement and impurities. The previous report has already recorded this. It is now heard that the institute's investigation shows that Shanghai wheat merchants have stockpiled more than 100,000 dan of inventory. If all of them are inspected, it seems that there will be no difficulties in terms of business sentiment. Therefore, based on the principle that the law does not investigate the past, and adopting the request of Ye Huijun, Chairman of the Shanghai Cereals Industry Association, the inventory transported before October 1st will be allowed to be registered, and no fees will be charged. Six temporary registration measures are specially formulated as follows: (1) All wheat inventory arriving before October 19th, 19th year of the Republic, will be allowed to be temporarily registered. (2) The registration date is from October 1st to October 5th. After the deadline, all will be treated as new goods and handled in accordance with the interim measures for inspecting wheat. (3) The registration location is the reporting and inspection office of this institute and the reporting and inspection branch office in Nanshi. (4) The applicant for registration shall fill in each item on the registration form prescribed by this institute and submit it to this institute together with the bill of lading to obtain a temporary registration certificate. (5) After obtaining a temporary registration certificate, when shipping goods, the institute shall be notified one day in advance to obtain a temporary pass for export or entry into the factory. The validity period of this temporary pass is set at two days, and it will be invalid if it expires. (6) If the quantity of the wheat inventory applying for registration is found to be inconsistent, or if new goods are used to impersonate inventory, etc., they will be punished in accordance with the regulations. The above articles have been officially notified to the Shanghai Municipal and Hansan Cereals Associations, respectively, to be forwarded to the wheat merchants for compliance.

Wu Song Rice Industry Workers Left Stores Yesterday

The workers of the entire Wu Song town's rice industry, due to the request of the capital to fulfill the conditions set by the Workers' Union, submitted a request to the Eighth District Party Department through the Wu Song District Branch to convene the capital to send three representatives to attend the district party department meeting to resolve the matter. The capital did not send representatives to attend the meeting, and the labor believed that the capital deliberately delayed and refused to fulfill the conditions. Therefore, yesterday, all the town's workers were convened to go to the district party department for a meeting. Yesterday morning, after the workers left the stores, no one supported the store affairs. Only the store owners maintained the market by themselves. Yesterday was the end-of-month settlement date, and there were no collection staff to collect rice accounts from the public. However, the remittances from various money houses and upper lines were urged very urgently, causing the owners of various firms to be very anxious. It is heard that the labor held a meeting and demanded that the capital agree to fulfill the conditions, otherwise they would have to wait for the resolution before they could enter the store to serve. It is estimated that there is no hope of a satisfactory solution today. The notice from the Rice and Grain Association and the notice from the Workers' Union are recorded below: (1) Notice: For urgent notice matters, it is now reported by the various firms of this association that the workers' union of this industry will hold a members' meeting at 7 am on September 30th. When the time comes, all colleagues will go to attend, and business will inevitably lack support. How should it be handled? Based on this, it is found that the workers of each firm should be allowed to leave the store to attend the members' meeting. As for business, it is hoped that the store owners and managers will temporarily support it to maintain the people's livelihood. This is hereby notified, Wu Song Rice and Grain Industry Association. (2) Notice: For notice matters, the Shanghai Rice Industry Workers' Union issued a letter stating that the Wu Song District Branch Executive Committee's request to fulfill the conditions was submitted to the Eighth District Party Department's Civil Training Committee for approval. After three convocations of representatives from both labor and capital to negotiate and proceed, the capital has repeatedly pushed back and delayed, and has not attended the meeting to negotiate earnestly, deliberately refusing to fulfill the agreed conditions, and destroying the agreed conditions. The cooperation between labor and capital in Wu Song is impossible. The capital uses stubborn means to deceive the workers, and it is obvious that it refuses the difficult and arduous requests. The branch should be aware of this and immediately convene a members' meeting to discuss methods and solutions to deal with it and extricate themselves. Approved. It is found that all members of this association in Wu Song have reached the extreme of hardship in their living conditions. The request for negotiation with the capital has resulted in such a result, which is very painful. This special urgent notice is hereby issued, and it is approved that a meeting of all members of the Wu Song Branch will be held in the auditorium of the District Party Department at 3 pm today. At that time, all members must attend. If any members are found to have declined to attend, the most severe warning will be given to emphasize discipline and there will be no leniency. Be sure to do so. The rest of the address is omitted.

Hengfeng Yarn Factory Workers Gradually Return to Work

At the Hengfeng Yarn Factory in Yangshupu, this city, on the 21st of this month, more than ten people, including weaving machine craftsmen and female supervisors, held a meeting outside and made some requests. Now, after investigation, the weaving machine craftsmen have gradually returned to work on the 27th. As for the female workers, it is expected that they will also be able to work as usual soon.

The Municipal Civil Training Committee Reprimands the Yarn Factory Industry Workers' Federation

The Mass Training Committee of the Executive Committee of this city yesterday issued an instruction and reprimanded the preparatory committee of the Yarn Factory Industry Workers' Federation for overstepping its authority by allowing Liu Hongxing and other workers' representatives from the Dafeng Yarn Factory to prepare to organize a trade union without first submitting it to the Party Department for approval. The original text of the Municipal Civil Training Committee's instruction is extracted as follows: "Report on submitting a report that Liu Hongxing and other workers from the Dafeng Yarn Factory have requested to organize a trade union, and the preparations have been ordered to proceed. A special report is hereby submitted for review and registration." The submitted documents have been received and understood. It is found that the association's authority is only responsible for guiding the trade unions in the industry, and it has no right to authorize the preparations for organizing and stopping the activities of various trade unions. In the past, it had repeatedly issued instructions and reprimanded the workers for organizing a trade union and stopping the activities of the Dongya Flax Bag Factory's trade union, and strictly ordered the association's instructor Xu Shaochuan to be on record. This time, they dared to allow the workers of the Dafeng Factory, Liu Hongxing and others, to prepare a trade union without authorization, which is extremely absurd and frivolous. It is similar to repeatedly violating discipline and overstepping.

The authority is really incorrigible and should be reprimanded. The request is not approved, and it is hoped that there will be no such behavior in the future. If it is committed again, it will be severely punished without leniency. Respect the order and do not violate it. This is of utmost importance. The original documents are returned, this order.

New Cigarette Tax Regulations Implemented Today

Abolishing the Seven-Level Tax System

Implementing the Three-Level Tax System on a Trial Basis

The new three-level tax collection regulations for the unified cigarette tax formulated by the Ministry of Finance have been approved by the Executive Yuan and will be implemented starting today (the 1st) for a three-month trial period. At the same time, the old seven-level tax collection regulations will be abolished. The new three-level tax system is divided into the following tax levels: Level 1, 220 yuan; Level 2, 56 yuan; Level 3, 32 yuan.

Opposing Water Rate Increases

Our association expresses its sympathy for this. According to reports, the company invited to audit the future budget, and the previous business reports were not involved. It can be seen that the company's intentions and methods are intended to exploit. If we let them exploit the citizens, there will be no survivors. Our association, as a group of citizens in the special district, has the responsibility to relieve the suffering of the citizens. After discussion by our special committee, no matter what the outcome of the audit, our association will always insist on the original plan to oppose the increase in prices and make further proposals. Water prices must have a certain standard and must not be calculated according to the amount of rent. The water fee income has exceeded several times the increase in rent over the years. Local News Two

Zhabei's Lights Went Out Last Night, Turning Into a Dark World

Generator Loses Vacuum

Temporary Power Supply from the Concession

Fortunately No Accidents Occurred in the Darkness

Normalcy Can Be Restored Today

Last night, the residents of Zhabei once again experienced the life of ten years ago, with dark streets, bleak and dim. After seven o'clock, shops closed their doors one after another, stopping business. The most prosperous Baoshan Road, Datong Road, and Hengfeng Road, etc., were different from usual. The streets were noisy with cars and horses, looking ahead and behind, fearing accidental collisions. From 6:30 pm to 8:45 pm, everyone hoped that the lights would be restored. The telephone of the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company rang continuously. Later, after the company contacted the Shanghai Electric Power Company of the Public Concession, the electricity from the concession was input to Zhabei, and the light was seen again for a short time. However, the sudden extinguishing of the lights was not due to the damage of the motor, but because the power plant in Yinhang Township, Wu Song, used a new machine, which had only been in use for two days. The workers were still inexperienced, so they accidentally lost the vacuum. As a result, the lights in the Zhabei area, except for those connected to the Fangpeng on Zhongshan Road, were all extinguished. Even the supply of tap water in Zhabei.

, was slightly affected at first.

The Reason for the Lights Going Out The electricity used in Zhabei was originally purchased by the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company from the Electricity Department of the former Public Concession, and then resold to users. Later, the Electricity Department was sold to the Shanghai Electric Power Company, and the electricity was still supplied as before. Until the day before yesterday, the company started using the new machine at the power plant in Yinhang Township, Wu Song, and cut off the live wire for power transmission. On the first day, the electricity generated by the plant was used to supply users, and the results were very good. Until yesterday afternoon around 6:30, when electricity was in great demand, the current suddenly interrupted, and the Zhabei area suddenly became a dark world. At first, it was thought that it could be repaired if there was a slight damage. Who knew that the users had waited for half an hour to 45 minutes, but the light still did not come. After hearing the news, the reporter was afraid that there was something else going on, so he drove to the Yinhang Township Power Plant to inquire. After engineer Chen Wenfu explained the reason for the lights going out, he suddenly realized that there were two Skeda generators in the power plant, each with a power of 10,000 kilowatts. The one currently in use is the second machine. The situation on the first day was very good. At about 6:30 last night, the generator suddenly lost its vacuum and lost its pulling force, and the motor stopped, and the current also stopped. This machine can probably work as usual today.

A Glimpse of Dark Zhabei There are two places in Fangpeng, which supplies electricity to Zhabei, one is at Junsong Bridge on Jungong Road, and the other is on Zhongshan Road. The former mainly supplies electricity to residents, such as Baoshan Road and Datong Road, etc., all of which are supplied by that place. The latter has relatively few users. The electricity used by factories near Zhongshan Road, etc., all comes from this Fangpeng. When the current stopped last night, all those belonging to the Junsong Bridge Fangpeng, whether it was electric lights or engines, were all extinguished and stopped. Those belonging to Zhongshan Road were not affected because there was still external electricity. Since the lights went out at about 6:30, the residents of Zhabei felt very inconvenient, because it was not long after the lights were turned on, and most of the households were preparing dinner. As soon as the lights went out, they could only grope in the dark. In addition, tap water was also temporarily suspended due to the current stopping and the motor being affected. With the water and electricity cut off, it was even more panic. The police chiefs of the fourth and fifth districts of Zhabei and all the public security bureaus were deeply afraid that villains would carry out activities in the dark, which would be detrimental to public security. Therefore, they immediately notified the police officers at each post to pay attention to prevention, and ordered the shops to close early to ensure safety. About ten minutes after the lights went out, the police at Post No. 15 on Gonghe Road in the jurisdiction of the Fourth District did capture a bandit with weapons in the dark and took him back to the district office for strict handling. However, during the dark period, the demand for candles and gas lamps was even more than the supply. The most embarrassed were the pedestrians on the road who were dressed in long gowns and carrying umbrellas. The rain was falling, and all around was dim, and they felt very embarrassed.

Li Mei Road

Robbery and Injury Last Night

Hongchang Pawnshop Suddenly Attacked by Violent Guests

The Boss Was Puffing Away

Calling for Catching Thieves Resulted in Being Shot and Injured

Detectives Arrested a Bandit

At 9:45 last night, Hongchang Pawnshop at No. 44 Li Mei Road in the French Concession was suddenly robbed, and the owner was shot and injured by the robbers. The loss was more than 2,000 yuan. One bandit was arrested on the spot. The details are recorded below:

The pawnshop is very remote Wang Zhaobo, a native of Pudong, 36 years old, has been operating Hongchang Pawnshop at No. 44 Li Mei Road in the French Concession for more than ten years. The scale is very small, but the location is remote and it is extremely quiet at night. Unexpectedly, it was coveted by bandits. At about 9:30 last night, when the pawnshop was preparing to close, three bandits in yellow and cyan raincoats suddenly came in one after another.

Three Thieves Burst in Armed The three thieves pretended to offer pawned items as a pretext to enter the door, pulled out their pistols, forced the buddies to open the gate, and rushed in. First, they drove the five people downstairs to the back of the hall, and then put all the cash in the drawer into the bag. One thief was left to monitor the people, and two thieves took the opportunity to go upstairs. At that time, the old manager Wang Zhaobo was puffing away on the back building, chatting with three relatives and friends. The thieves broke in with guns.

Calling for Robbers Resulted in Being Shot and Injured The owner Wang knew he had encountered robbers, but was intimidated by the power of the thieves and dared not speak out. The two thieves turned over boxes and cabinets, and used iron tools to pry open the wooden box for storing money. All the money in the box was robbed. Just as they were about to leave with the stolen goods, Wang was about to get up and call for catching thieves, and a robber fired a shot, hitting his back shoulder and piercing his front arm. Wang fell down in pain, bleeding all over the bed.

One Thief Fled into a Noodle Shop When the three thieves had obtained the stolen goods and fled out of the door, the store buddies shouted wildly for catching thieves. Nearby police whistles sounded loudly, and a little south of the pawnshop was Huage Nao Road, the residences of Du Yuesheng and Zhang Xiaolin. The bodyguards gathered after hearing the alarm and searched in all directions. A thief saw that the situation was not good, and in his hurry, he cleverly fled into Yongxingguan Noodle Shop at No. 50 next door, hoping to hide and escape.

Detectives Arrested a Thief At the same time, the detectives also rushed to the scene after hearing the alarm. They found the thief's face flustered, and the detectives captured him and took him to the police station. They went to the pawnshop to inspect the scene. The thieves abandoned a six-inch Brown Lin pistol with four bullets in it in their haste to escape. Boss Wang was taken to Renji Hospital by car. It is said that although the injuries were not serious, Wang suffered from hemoptysis, and the excessive bleeding has caused serious damage to his body. The Shanghai community is raising money.

Further Hearing of You Yaho's Lawsuit Against Her Husband for Bigamy

You Fails to Appear Due to Childbirth

Yang Xuejiu's Illness Has Not Yet Healed

Zhang Nai Will Return Home Soon

You's Mother Testifies in Court Yesterday

Yang Xuejiu, the principal of a girls' school in Chengdong, was sued for criminal bigamy by Zhang Nai's (Yu Xuelou) first wife, You Yaho, after she married Zhang. Zhang's mother and sister, as well as Yang's mother, were all implicated. Except for Zhang, who is still in Japan, Yang has been brought to court for questioning and ordered to be released on bail. However, when the court reopened, Yang claimed to be ill again and did not appear. The judge ordered her to be brought in. These details have been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, when the hearing was scheduled to resume, many relatives and friends from both sides arrived at the Second Court of the Special District Court, mostly women, who came specifically to observe. However, the plaintiff, You Yaho, was unable to attend due to her recent joy of giving birth on the 25th of last month and her physical weakness after childbirth, and she is recuperating at Guangren Hospital. Yang Xuejiu also claimed to be ill and did not attend, and lawyer Yan Jiang represented her. The other defendants also did not attend, but You's mother represented her daughter in court. You's mother is old, with gray hair, but her speech is very elegant. According to You's mother, the last time the photographer proved that Zhang and Yang's wedding photo was taken, it was a joint criminal act between the two of them, which has been established. Now, the witness and physical evidence are complete and should be punished according to the law. Judge Cheng asked if there was any other evidence. You's mother replied that there was a lot of evidence, but it was all lost. Moreover, when Zhang Nai was in mourning for his parents, Yang Xuejiu sent a eulogy, and Zhang's obituary also mentioned that he was married. Therefore, Yang actually knew that Zhang Nai was a married man, not a widower. When Yang was detained in the police station, she asked my daughter why she was dissatisfied with Zhang and expressed that she could mediate. This shows that Yang's relationship with Zhang was very close. As for Zhang's whereabouts, he is not actually in Japan. He is probably at his sister's house or in Hangzhou. She requested that he be arrested and brought to justice. My daughter is currently recuperating in the hospital after childbirth, but she has no money and is extremely poor. To support her in raising her child, she should be given financial assistance. This issue concerns the Zhang family's ancestral shrine, so please summon Zhang's mother, Yu Zhangshi, to resolve it properly. Then, lawyer Jiang stated that Yang was indeed suffering from illness and did not intentionally fail to appear. She will appear in court next time. Zhang Nai is also said to be returning to China from Japan. Judge Cheng then ordered the police to strictly arrest Zhang Nai and ordered the guarantor to bring Yang Xuejiu to court. The hearing was postponed for fourteen days.

Zhu Ziyun Has Gone to Hangzhou for Recuperation After Escaping Danger

Zhu Escaped for Sixty Yuan

The Bandits in Caihua Lane Are Nowhere to Be Found

The Landlord Couple Is Detained

Each Sentenced to Post a Bail of Three Thousand Yuan

Zhu Ziyun, a throat specialist, was kidnapped by bandits and hidden on a boat. It was not until the afternoon of the 28th of last month that Zhu suddenly escaped. After returning home, Zhu immediately reported to the Harbin Police Station, saying that on the morning of the 20th of last month, he was kidnapped by bandits from his residence at 3151 Zhoujiazui Road and taken to Caihua Lane, 722 Qipu Road, by car. He was dragged into the house, and the bandits sprayed a kind of potion on his face and wrapped his eyes with a towel. He immediately fell into a coma. The next morning at 3:00 AM, he was moved by the bandits to a small boat in Rihui Port in West Shanghai and hidden, with two bandits guarding him. On the afternoon of the 28th, when one of the bandits left the boat to go ashore, he promised the other bandit sixty yuan and was able to escape. The police chief immediately sent detective Zhu Hanbo and detective Yan Shiqing to investigate Caihua Lane, 722. The so-called kidnappers had already fled. However, the landlord of the house, Fei Zhenkun, a Chongming native, and his wife, Zhu, rented out the remaining rooms as a bandit's den, and they also deserved to be blamed. Chinese and Western detectives arrested the Fei couple. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Special District Court, where Judge Ge Zitan interrogated them. Detective Zhu reported on the investigation and said that Zhu's escape, according to his telephone call, was due to promising the guard bandit sixty yuan to be released. The truth is still unclear, and Zhu has not yet appeared in court. Zhu's agent lawyer, Lu Qi, stated that Zhu was overly frightened after returning from the bandit's den, resulting in illness, and has now gone to Hangzhou for recuperation, entrusting his brother, Zhu Zhongyun, to represent him in court. Zhu Zhongyun then stated that on the day of the incident, three or four kidnappers suddenly came to his brother's medical residence, each holding a pistol, dragged his brother out, forced him onto a car prepared by the bandits in front of the door, and drove away quickly. The bandits were all young and wore black short clothes. After his brother was kidnapped, the bandits did not send any words, but before the incident, his brother had received two threatening letters demanding three thousand yuan, which his brother ignored. After his brother returned, he said that although his eyes were covered when he was taken to Caihua Lane and his vision was lost, he could still hear the bandits talking, mixed with Ningbo, Chongming, Jiangbei, and other accents. Fei Zhu and his wife testified that they had only rented in Caihua Lane for two months. The house was a two-story building. The Fei couple lived behind the hall, and the upstairs was intended to be rented out. On the 19th of the lunar July, a man and woman with Ningbo accents claimed to be a couple and came to rent the remaining rooms. The man said his name was Jin and he was in the rice business. They agreed on a rent of twenty yuan per month. When they moved in on the 21st, another man came with them, claiming to be his brother. The man was in his thirties, wearing a Western suit, and had a fair complexion. The person claiming to be Jin had pockmarks and a red complexion and was in his forties. The woman was only in her twenties and had a small square face, also with a red complexion. They moved out at the end of the month. According to the woman, she used to work as a maid in a rice store and became acquainted with this man named Jin. Jin had a wife, and his wife had found out about them and was afraid of causing trouble, so they moved to avoid her. When the two men and one woman moved out on the third day of the eighth lunar month, they did not know where they went. When they lived in their house, they did not see any hostages, nor did they know if they were bandits. Fei Zhenkun's statement was similar to Zhu's. Judge Ge then ordered the two defendants to each post a bail of three thousand yuan. If they could not provide bail, they would be detained separately, and the hearing would be adjourned for further investigation.

South Shanghai Traffic Connection

The Shanghai-Minhang-Nanzhe Long-Distance Company on Guohuo Road in Nanshi, Shanghai, has seen its business develop rapidly since the opening of the Shanghai-Minhang route. However, the Nanzhe route across the river, although the roadbed has been built by the Nanhuifengxian Construction Bureaus respectively, the bridges are still being planned and are not yet open to traffic. Therefore, the transportation between Nanfeng cannot be connected with Shanghai-Minhang, which is deeply inconvenient for local merchants and residents. At the moment, gentry and merchants from all walks of life in Nanqiao have initiated the establishment of the Yongxin Steamship Company, purchasing three of the latest type of steamships, which are scheduled to depart from Nanqiao at 7:00 AM every day starting from October 1st, heading to Minhang, and departing from Minhang to Nanqiao in the afternoon. In addition to applying for the protection of the Fengxian County Government's announcement, it has also been agreed with the Shanghai-Minhang Company to connect with long-distance buses each time and issue joint tickets. Therefore, the transportation between South Shanghai is connected in one go, and travelers are praising it.

The internal work, such as the girls, family, children, general education, dormitory, labor, introduction, and other departments, are all working hard to improve and strive to meet the needs of society. Moreover, because more and more women in Shanghai are joining the business world, preparations are now being made to seek the development of the four educations for women in the business world. In addition to the Women's Workers' Society on Xiaoshadu Road, the labor department will also set up a women's workers' district and a women's workers' dormitory on Robertson Road. As for the house on Nanjing Road, it will take time to equip it, and it will not be possible to move in until early November. This women's service organization with more than twenty years of history in Shanghai will surely shine with innovation.

Record of the Qianyi Hospital Board Meeting

The Red Cross Qianyi Hospital held its sixth anniversary board meeting at the Yueqiao Commercial Federation on Laobazi Road at 3:00 PM on the 27th of this month. Those present included General Director Chen Bingqian, President Wang Binyan, Directors Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, Wang Xiaolai, Qin Runqing, Yu Zongzhou, Zhu Yiqian, Tong Zhonglian, etc. The meeting was held as usual, with General Director Chen Bingqian presiding and Zhu Yiqian recording. President Wang reported on the state of the association's affairs, saying that the hospital specializes in providing medical treatment and medicine. Within the past nineteen and a half years, it has treated more than 300 people with serious bone fractures, more than 500 people with bone fractures, and more than 20,000 people with common diseases. More than 11,000 unregistered people were introduced by various military police groups, philanthropists, and directors. The medical service has doubled compared with last year, and in terms of funding, it has been slightly more spacious since Director Du Yuesheng generously donated 300 yuan per month for rent last year. In addition, the hospital received a total of 9,695.40 yuan in registration fees, hospitalization fees, and donations from various directors and patients who were cured. In terms of expenses, the total expenditure was 10,782.72 yuan, which was not much different from the income. This achievement is all due to the enthusiastic maintenance and loving care of Director Du Yuesheng and Director Qin Runqing, which made it possible. After the report was completed, it was decided by the directors to look for land and build a new hospital in order to expand it, considering that the hospital site had expired and needed to be demolished.

Tragic Record of a Poor Woman Starving to Death

The Child Is Taken in by the Station

A woman surnamed Zhang lived on Xinjia Road in North Shanghai. Her husband was sentenced to prison for smoking opium. The woman took her eight-year-old child and wandered outside. She had no money, was sick, had no house to live in, and no food to eat. She slept under the overpass in Xinkangli and starved to death after not eating or drinking for three days. The child was also unable to speak, so his name was unknown. The matter was learned by the Third Section of the Fifth District. In addition to keeping the child at the station, the land guarantee was ordered yesterday to report to the court for examination and to the newspaper for collection.

Two People Committed Suicide by Swallowing Opium

Zhou Azhao, the wife of a tailor living at 121 Yinyuli, Baxianqiao, French Concession, was 26 years old and from Ningbo. They had been married for several years and had a very deep affection. However, A's father was addicted to alcohol, and her father was also addicted to opium. Both fathers-in-law lived with A. His wife, seeing that her husband's productivity was weak and the economy was gradually strained, suddenly had suicidal thoughts yesterday afternoon and swallowed raw opium in secret. People noticed and sent her to Renji Hospital for treatment, but she took too much poison and died at 6:00 PM that night.

Liu Dezhi, a native of Shandong, was 24 years old and had been engaged in the flour paper business, often traveling between Yantai and Shanghai. He came to Shanghai from Yantai in June and lived in the Dongjuchang Customs Brokerage on the Bund. Recently, he became involved in gambling dens and brothels, spending more than 2,000 yuan. His capital was gradually strained, and the landlord in Yantai sent a letter urging him to pay the debt. Liu was at a loss and could not find a way to make money. He suddenly committed suicide and swallowed raw opium yesterday morning. Because the rescue was not timely, he died at 7:00 PM that night.

Sino-Japanese Telecommunications Conference Postponed

Japanese Commissioners Did Not Go to Beijing Yesterday

Due to Problems Still to Be Discussed

The third meeting of the Sino-Japanese telecommunications negotiations was originally scheduled to be held in Beijing today (1st). The Japanese commissioners, Shigekitsu and Yoshino, were originally scheduled to go to Beijing yesterday to attend the meeting. However, the Japanese commissioners suddenly suspended their trip to Beijing yesterday for some reason. Therefore, the meeting today may not be held. According to news from the Japanese Embassy Office yesterday, the third meeting of the Sino-Japanese telecommunications negotiations has been contacted by the Sino-Japanese commissioners several times. It was originally scheduled to be held in Beijing today. However, because two meetings were held a few days ago, all the procedures and other procedures have been negotiated. This meeting must negotiate the main body of the negotiations. The first step is to negotiate the sea line between Shanghai and Nagasaki. This line is the most important part of the Sino-Japanese telecommunications negotiations and is of great importance. It is not easy to negotiate without a specific plan first. At present, there are still various problems and incidental problems that need to be discussed by the two commissioners before they can be formally negotiated. Moreover, the Japanese commissioners currently have differences with the Chinese commissioners on the fixed position of the Shanghai-Nagasaki line. Therefore, they still need to exchange personal opinions first. Therefore, the meeting today may have to be postponed for a day or two before it can be convened again.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce's Appeal for Taxing People's Food

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday, at the request of the Chinese Merchants' Grain, Oil, and Cake Association and the Guangzhou Rice Merchants' Association, telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, earnestly requesting the abolition of food taxes. The two telegrams are recorded below: (1) Please Exempt Hunan Rice from Transit Tax to the Nanjing Ministry of Finance. According to a letter from the Municipal Chinese Merchants' Grain, Oil, and Cake Association, a letter was received from the Shanghai Bean and Rice Industry Association and the Han Produced Grain Industry Association, stating that Hunan rice has never been subject to heavy taxes when it arrives in Hankou. Now, the Hankou Customs is actually collecting Hunan rice transit tax, one yuan per catty, which affects people's food and causes public panic. They requested that the Ministry of Finance be forwarded to order the Hankou Customs to withdraw its order to maintain the people's food in the interior. I believe that the harvest was poor last year, and rice prices soared, making it difficult for common people to support themselves. Therefore, they have ordered foreign rice one after another to provide assistance. The outflow of money is countless. Our country is known as an agricultural country, but there is such a huge loophole, which is not heartbreaking. Fortunately, this year's harvest is abundant, and it is expected that rice prices will become cheaper day by day to relieve the people's plight. However, the Hankou Customs is actually collecting Hunan rice transit tax. It is heard that Hunan Province is the richest rice-producing area, and the lower reaches of the Yangtze River and the northern provinces and cities rely on it for food. Then, the source of Hunan rice is abundant and has a great impact on the people's food in the north and south. Now, it is heard that the Hankou Customs is actually collecting this kind of transit tax, which amounts to one yuan per hundred catties. Each stone is calculated at one hundred and forty catties, which is one yuan and four jiao. In addition, there are transportation costs, water freight, etc., which increases the cost sharply and makes transportation and sales difficult. Rice merchants will inevitably stop moving forward, so how can Hunan rice be exported? This is tantamount to cutting off the food source for the northern and southern provinces. Last year's poor harvest and soaring rice prices can still be attributed to unfavorable weather. Now, the Hankou Customs is collecting this transit tax, increasing the cost of Hunan rice, which will raise rice prices and lead to food difficulties for the people. Where should the blame lie? In the case of a poor harvest and high prices, the authorities should try to suppress them. The Hankou Customs is levying taxes on Hunan rice because of the abundant harvest, raising its cost and oppressing the people's food. Is this what a benevolent person would want to do? The matter concerns the inland grain, so I dare not remain silent. I dare to forward the situation to the Ministry of Finance and ask you to quickly order the Hankou Customs to cancel the order for the Hunan rice transit tax, so that there will be endless benefits to the common people. I have come here with such feelings. I believe that in recent years, agricultural production has been poor and rice prices have soared, and the people's food difficulties have reached the extreme. However, the Hankou Customs is actually collecting Hunan rice transit taxes during the abundant harvest, amounting to one yuan per hundred catties, creating an unprecedentedly harsh levy that affects the supply of food to the north and south. I am afraid that it will harm the people's livelihood and foster hidden dangers. The facts stated are indeed true, and it is reasonable to telegraph your department and ask you to order the Hankou Customs to exempt the special tax in order to maintain the people's food, which is a truly virtuous act. (2) Please Exempt Guangdong Rice Merchants from Stamp Duty

The original telegram stated briefly that on September 27, representatives Zhang Tiejun and Li Futian of the Guangzhou Rice Merchants' Association and Chen Shuoshi, representative of the Guangzhou Rice and Grain Distribution Industry Association, jointly wrote a letter stating that Guangdong Province has always suffered from insufficient food supply. Recently, grain and rice prices have been rising, and they have to rely on foreign rice from abroad to make up for it. Recently, the gold is expensive and the silver is cheap, and the impact is such that it is difficult to calculate the import of grain and rice. Moreover, it is difficult to resist the sale of foreign ships, and bankruptcy is often heard. Although merchants and residents are trying their best to purchase, the cost is high and the stockpiles are small. In addition, there have been frequent water and drought disasters, and famine is often heard. This is a hidden worry for the future of the Guangdong Province food supply. The government should maintain the people's food and exempt the additional tax on food in order to reduce the burden on the common people. In the old days of the late Qing Dynasty, the import tax on rice in Guangdong Province was generally exempted. After the establishment of the Republic of China, the stamp duty was also repeatedly approved by the former Finance Minister and Governor Hu to exempt rice and grain from stamp duty. Today, the standard of living is increasing day by day, the people's livelihood is deteriorating day by day, and the price of rice is much higher than before. Now, with the burden of stamp duty, the pain is unbearable. Stamp duty is a national tax law, but in order to maintain the people's food, it has been exempted by the government in the past. How can it be re-imposed in the future? Our association and others, for the sake of the people's food, cannot remain silent. We hereby ask your association to verify and earnestly ask you to forward it to the Ministry of Finance to consider the lack of food in Guangdong Province, approve the exemption of stamp duty on commercial documents for grain and rice in Guangdong, in order to maintain the people's food and care for the merchants' difficulties. According to this, Guangdong Province has been suffering from years of disasters and poor harvests, and rice prices have been rising. It has to rely on foreign rice to provide relief. The tax authorities charge stamp duty on the import documents of the foreign rice, which increases the cost and raises the selling price. The impact on the general poor people is significant. Therefore, the former Guangdong Province authorities had a precedent of exempting rice and grain from stamp duty. Now, rice prices are rising more and more sharply. One yuan can only buy six or seven catties of rice. It is appropriate to follow the previous case and exempt the stamp duty in order to lighten the burden. It is reasonable to telegraph your department for verification, approve and order the Guangdong Province finance authorities to continue to exempt the stamp duty according to the previous case in order to relieve the people's food.

China Bank Inspection Report

Thirty-First Time

The thirty-first inspection report of the Shanghai China Bank Issuance Reserve Inspection Committee states: The members of this committee, along with the entrusted accountants, based on the rules of this committee, inspected the Shanghai China Bank's issuance and affiliated branches' designated reserve vault for exchange notes. The thirty-first inspection was conducted at the bank on September 28th of the 19th year of the Republic of China, with the participation of the Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance. The results of the inspection are listed below: The total amount of exchange note issuance is 121,746,496 yuan, three jiao, and five fen, including: The bank's issuance amount is 61,512,336 yuan and two jiao, the affiliated branches' borrowing amount is 27,902,336 yuan, one jiao, and five fen, and the various banks and firms' borrowing amount is 32,331,824 yuan. Except for the portion borrowed by various banks and firms, which will be inspected separately according to the original method, this inspection covers the affiliated branches' portion as follows: The bank's issuance and affiliated branches' borrowing amount is 89,414,672 yuan, three jiao, and five fen. The reserve amount for exchange notes of this affiliated branch is 89,414,672 yuan, three jiao, and five fen, including: Cash reserve amount is 53,632,222 yuan and nine jiao and three fen, and the guarantee reserve amount is 55,762,449 yuan and four jiao and two fen. The above two items total: the cash reserve accounts for 60% of the total, and the guarantee reserve accounts for 40% of the total. All amounts were checked without error. In accordance with Article 5 of the rules, this is a formal report. September 28th, 19th year of the Republic of China. Xu Kan, Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance; Wang Yansong, Pei Yunqing, representatives of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce; Xu Xinliu, Hu Mengjia, representatives of the Shanghai Bankers' Association; Yan Junan, Shen Yisheng, representatives of the Shanghai Money Dealers' Association; Le Gengrong, Zhou Jiefan, representatives of the note-receiving banks and firms; Chen Guangfu, Li Zhilian, Xu Jiqing, Ye Zhuotang, Zhou Zongliang, representatives of the directors and supervisors of the China Bank; Wang Zikang, Accountant.
